Commentary

Saving the Crisis of the Spinning Industry

— Respectfully

China's textile industry is the earliest to take on a modern industrial form, a common characteristic of emerging industrial nations and a universal phenomenon of global progress. However, since the global economic panic of 1929, China's economy has been pressured externally by the raging tide of the depression and internally by the limited market. Outward exports have been hampered by tariff barriers, while domestically there has been intense competition from imported goods. Therefore, even though the industry has done its best to implement various measures such as reducing work and limiting production quantities, it has ultimately failed to achieve any effect and has only deteriorated further. The hope for rising yarn prices remains elusive, and the stockpiles in warehouses remain difficult to clear. Thus, the crisis of the entire cotton yarn industry has intensified. If there are no practical and appropriate relief measures, the future will face the same fate as the silk industry.

However, if we want to discuss relief, we must first explore the source of the yarn industry's crisis. From the perspective of the overall economic situation, every industry in the world shows signs of decline. The textile industry, such as Lancashire in England, is also experiencing unusual decline. China is naturally no exception. But the main reason is still the increasingly shrinking yarn market. Since 1929, countries around the world have leaned toward economic self-sufficiency, minimizing the import of foreign products and increasing domestic exports. From the home country to the colonies, all are trying to manage the consumption of our cotton products. Although it cannot reach the world, there is still room to maneuver in the Nanyang region. However, recently, it has been affected by the poor local market and by the intense pressure of Japanese products. As a result, overseas consumption has been reduced to zero. At the same time, foreign products have invaded our domestic market, causing us to lose our superior position in the country. Moreover, foreigners invest and set up factories in China, taking advantage of their sophisticated technology and our cheap labor. All geographical advantages are shared with us, and they have taken the lead in industrial operation, product production, and transportation. This is another main cause of the crisis.

Is it possible that China's yarn factories, with the convenience of low labor costs and the benefit of local production and consumption, cannot compete with others? The output of yarn factories is affected by negative political and economic factors, such as heavy taxes and excessive transportation costs, which are enough to make China's cotton yarn lag behind foreign products. In times of better economic conditions, it can barely be maintained. Once external forces strike, it will immediately be in trouble. In addition, although many of those who operate yarn factories in China are able to use modern methods, they still follow past habits. It is feared that some factories are bureaucratic. Such factories have huge expenditures and poor work performance, and their output is even below average. They cannot compete with strong enemies in peacetime, let alone in this era of intensified economic competition. For now, the spinning industry must be thoroughly aware of the current crisis in order to save it. First, it must seek rationalization of operations and eliminate accumulated habits. Second, it must carefully investigate the relationship between domestic and foreign markets and strive to recover the lost market in the shortest possible time.

China is originally a vast world market, sufficient to absorb huge quantities of commodities. Our industry has plenty of room for development. But why has the entire national economy been so devastated? The lives of the masses are in a state of upheaval and ruin. Therefore, whether we want to seek a temporary small-scale prosperity in the economic sector today or find a way out for an industry, we must first pay attention to the state of the entire national economy in order to determine the strategy to deal with it. If the yarn industry wants to develop consumption at home and this type of consumption's expansion, it must first seek to stabilize the national economy and increase the consumption of general daily necessities. Then the yarn industry will naturally benefit. Moreover, China's production and consumption should be mainly based on the vast majority of farmers. Actively revitalizing the rural economy is also indirectly creating a market for the cotton yarn industry.

Fascist Leaders Compete to Lead the World; Reconstructing Europe is an Urgent Task; The Venice Talks Are Secret; Reportedly Agreed to Help Germany Achieve Military Equality in Exchange for a Truce on the Austrian Issue; Yesterday Morning, They Reviewed the Pan-Fascist Party Army; Afternoon, A Conference on Gunboats

Venice Today, Prime Minister Mussolini and German Chancellor Hitler met for the first time, speaking in German for two hours and twenty-five minutes. No third party participated. They explained their mutual political attitudes to each other. This conversation was purely an exchange of information. The two leaders will continue their talks tomorrow when they cruise on the waters of Venice. Conclusions can only be reached after a second talk in the evening. The press believes that since Germany and Poland have been able to reconcile on the Danzig issue, the Austrian issue may also be resolved peacefully. (Havas dispatch, 14th)

Venice The two giants of Italy and Germany are meeting here today. Prime Minister Mussolini acted swiftly and began negotiations with Chancellor Hitler. He is urging the German Chancellor to return to Geneva in order to fully implement the Four-Power Pact. (National Telegram, 14th)

Venice The nature of the talks between the Italian and German Chancellors remains strictly confidential and has not been disclosed. According to rumors, the Italian Prime Minister intends to allow Italy to mediate so that Germany can honorably return to the League of Nations and obtain military equality. The Italian Prime Minister will ask Germany for a truce on the Austrian issue as a reward.

Venice After reviewing the Pan-Fascist Party Army this morning, Mussolini and Hitler jointly attended a banquet hosted by the Italian government. After the banquet, the two prime ministers will take a speedboat to the village of Murano by the lake to begin their second political consultation. A welcome rally will be held in St. Mark's Square tonight, and Mussolini is expected to deliver a speech. It is predicted that this speech will be a major political event. (Havas dispatch, 14th)

St. Mark's Square; Review of the Pan-Fascist Party Army; Black Shirts Form a Long Snake Array; Japanese Royal Family Member Hezhou Also Participates in the Review

Venice Today, German Chancellor Hitler and Italian Prime Minister Mussolini stood together on the reviewing stand to review the Fascist troops and all units. Three thousand people were reviewed. The review location was in the historically famous St. Mark's Square. Present were stormtroopers, youth groups, and other teams, lined up in a long array of black shirts. The troops gave the Fascist salute, and Hitler responded with the National Socialist Party salute. (National Telegram, 15th)

Venice Japanese royal family member Hezhou Gong and his wife arrived here today from Florence with a secretary from the Japanese Embassy. When Prime Minister Mussolini and German Chancellor Hitler jointly review the Pan-Fascist Party Army tomorrow, Hezhou Gong and his wife will also participate. (Havas dispatch, 14th)

Venice This afternoon, Italian Prime Minister Mussolini and German Chancellor Hitler will meet again on a gunboat. The boat will cruise outside Lido, and another 20 warships will be distributed nearby.

The First Meeting of the Two Leaders

Yesterday, the two dictators met at the Villa Pisani after lunch to discuss important European affairs. It lasted two and a half hours, and there was no third person in the room, so the true nature of the conversation is not expected to be leaked. This is Hitler's first trip abroad since taking office as Chancellor and also his first meeting with Italian Prime Minister Mussolini.

The Content of the Conversation is Kept Secret

There is no news about the conversation, so the general public is very concerned about whether the two dictators have reached an agreement. They both seem to admire each other. When they shook hands, it lasted a long time and their expressions were sincere. The conversation was in German, as Mussolini is also proficient in this language.

Like the Triumphant Return of Ancient Heroes

Yesterday, when Hitler and Mussolini entered Venice together, it was like the triumphant return of two heroes of the ancient republic. The magnificent scenery of the Middle Ages was seen again today. When Hitler landed from the plane, Mussolini immediately gave the Fascist salute, and Hitler returned the National Socialist Party salute. The two then spoke in German for a few minutes. Then, they boarded a small boat and entered Venice along the canal, followed by countless small boats, like a long snake advancing. Upon arriving in the ancient city, the Italians enthusiastically cheered for their Prime Minister, while the Germans gathered outside the grand hotel where Hitler was staying and cheered "Long live Hitler." The authorities took strict precautions to protect this distinguished guest and stationed police and soldiers to guard the hotel.

The Scheduled Program Has Been Changed

The scheduled program has been slightly changed. Mussolini did not spend the night at the Villa Pisani but stayed at the luxurious hotel in Lido, which is a popular place in the summer but is not yet open. It is said that the two prime ministers only exchanged opinions yesterday, and a decision may be made during today's meeting. Last night, Mussolini went to the grand hotel to return Hitler's visit. The two then walked out side by side, and their relationship seemed very harmonious.

Involves the Issue of Austrian Independence

Political sources in Vienna now believe that Hitler will be more accommodating to Mussolini's views on the issue of Austrian independence.

Lanterns on the Water Welcome the Distinguished Guests

A lantern festival was held on the Grand Canal last night, with 200 illuminated boats participating, which was very grand and showed the intention of welcoming distinguished guests.

Venice is Heavily Guarded

Now, anyone entering the grand hotel where Hitler and others are staying must obtain a pass from the authorities and be admitted based on the pass. Those without passes are prohibited from entering. Hidden cannons are placed around the port of Venice, and two machine guns are placed on the watchtowers, guarded day and night. The strictness of the security is evident. (Reuters dispatch, 15th)

Britain and France Closely Monitor

(London) Political circles here are closely monitoring the meeting between Hitler and Mussolini. Newspapers have published long articles commenting on the matter, calling it a historical meeting. The Morning Post said that Mussolini hoped to eliminate the dangers of the global arms race after the failure of the Disarmament Conference. (National Telegram, 14th)

(London) The London Times' Venice dispatch today claimed that the meeting between the Italian and German Chancellors was welcomed because it told the world that Germany was not isolated in Europe. Italian Prime Minister Mussolini has always held the belief that European peace can only be guaranteed by actions based on the basic principles of the Four-Power Pact. Even the Far East situation has caused unnecessary disputes because the major European powers cannot resolve their differences. The general Italian population still believes that Mussolini's plan to restore commercial prosperity in Central Europe is the only feasible solution and that it should both preserve Austria's integrity and give Germany some of the political influence and commercial benefits it deserves. It is hoped that Mussolini can persuade Hitler to adopt a friendly attitude towards Austria, and Mussolini may provide the German Chancellor with new assistance on the issue of military equipment. (Reuters dispatch, 15th)

(Paris) French newspapers have expressed deep interest in the meeting between Hitler and Mussolini. One newspaper said that there may be nothing to hide in the meeting, and the topics of discussion will not go beyond the European situation. (National Telegram, 14th)

German and Italian Newspaper Opinions: Both Countries Do Not Wish to Sign Any Treaties, Hoping Four-Power Cooperation Will Benefit European Peace

(Berlin) German newspapers tonight reported that the meeting between Chancellor Hitler and Prime Minister Mussolini was not a signal of a sudden turn in German foreign policy. Chancellor Hitler's trip to Italy will not cause political upheaval in foreign countries, as there are no plans to sign any formal treaties in Venice. Hitler and Mussolini merely want to discuss all complex political issues. For example, the fault for the unresolved Austrian issue lies with Austria. (National Telegram, 14th)

Rome. The Rome News published an article today, expressing the enthusiastic welcome for the visit of German Chancellor Hitler. The newspaper said, "Mr. Hitler is not only a distinguished guest from a neighboring country who should be given the highest honor and the warmest welcome, but he is also a person who controls destiny. He has an unstoppable spirit and unwavering confidence, so he can make the people of the whole country sincerely embrace him and recast Germany, uniting with the national socialist banner." The newspaper continued, saying that it is especially meaningful that the two leaders have chosen this time to meet, because the recent passage of the disarmament conference resolution is of no benefit to the European situation, and no matter what kind of resolution is to be effective for a long time, maintain European peace, and protect the future of Europe, it must have Germany's participation. This is now an unquestionable fact. Therefore, the meeting between Hitler and Mussolini today is of great importance. The chaos in the European diplomatic community can be temporarily calmed down. Germany's return to Geneva is a permanent issue, and it is difficult to find a suitable solution unless it is based on justice and humanity. Only Benito Mussolini can say a word to clarify the European situation and promote world peace and cooperation. (National Telegram, 14th)

The Roman Tribune welcomed Chancellor Hitler, saying that Fascist Italy recognizes the historical status requested by Germany and respects Chancellor Hitler as the leader of the liberation movement in Germany. The liberation completed by Hitler is a part of the reconstruction of Europe. This kind of transformation alone is enough to restore Europe's spirit of guiding the world, and this spirit is also what Mussolini advocates. Those who oppose Mussolini and Hitler must observe their meeting from this point of view. The urgent task in Europe is for countries to have stable and responsible governments in order to cope with our problems. The Italian Daily News stated that the meeting between Hitler and Mussolini is a manifestation of the power of peace and clearing up chaos. The European situation is now very difficult and full of crises, such as the failure of disarmament, the revival of the arms race, the rise of bloc politics, and the hope of suppressing extremists to prolong the economic panic, etc. Therefore, stability is impossible. Mussolini opposes bloc politics and is loyal to the cooperation method of the Four-Power Pact. The Four-Power Peace Pact is the ideal cornerstone of European order and peace. (National Telegram, 14th)

Russian Planes Formations Reconnoiter Over Mishan

(Harbin) According to official sources, three Russian military planes flew over Mishan County on the Russian-Manchurian border today, and then formed a formation and flew east into Russian territory. When reconnaissance of Mishan was required, its height was about 1,500 meters. (Reuters, 15th)

France Increases Expenses to Strengthen National Defense: The Government Submits to the House of Representatives for Discussion; Prime Minister Doumergue Recalls the Lessons of the European War, Saying That He Cannot Sit Back and Watch Neighboring Countries Grow Their Wings; The Socialist Party's Motion to Postpone Discussion Is Rejected

(Paris) On March 10 this year, the government submitted a draft law on national defense expenditures to the House of Representatives, with a total expenditure of 2,980,000,000 francs for the army, navy, and air force. Later, because the border defense project was to be completed quickly and construction encountered difficulties, it was increased to 3,120,000,000 francs. This case was fully approved by the House of Representatives Finance Committee on June 6 by 22 votes to 12. Today, the House of Representatives met to discuss this case. The orthodox socialist party first raised a preliminary question. The government proposed a vote of confidence to show its opposition. The House of Representatives finally rejected the socialist party's proposal by a majority of 472 votes to 125. At this point, the rapporteur stood up to report, saying that the government's bill included three items: (1) Construction of border defense projects, (2) Construction of naval liquid fuel storage facilities, (3) Allowing the Air Force to act in conjunction with the Army and Navy. Army Minister General Petain explained from a technical point of view the necessity of disbursing funds to protect the safety of residents. The Socialist Party also requested that the national defense expenditure case be postponed for discussion. Prime Minister Doumergue strongly opposed it. In the end, the Socialist Party's postponement proposal was rejected by a majority of 459 votes to 125. Prime Minister Doumergue gave a speech, recalling past lessons, saying that before 1914, he was responsible for renovating fortresses in the areas of Nancy and the Gomuz Mountains. During the war, that place never fell into the hands of the enemy. The Prime Minister also said that past history, in short, is "We French were attacked, but we also struggled to defend ourselves. The past of the European War is like this." Since the end of the European War, France has shortened the length of military service, while foreign countries have secretly reorganized their military equipment at a rapid pace. The disarmament conference is working in Geneva, but some countries believe that it is of no value. In October 1932, the current German Chancellor sent an open letter to former Prime Minister von Papen, saying that international conferences only ratify what has already been done, and said, "Germany's rearmament or France's reduction of armaments, in our view, is the same thing. In conclusion, rearmament lies in Germany's own efforts and cannot be sought from Geneva. Once Germany's military equipment is completed, the situation will be a fait accompli. What can the international community do to me? Otherwise, it is difficult to hope for the recognition of the disarmament conference." This is the German side's argument. Therefore, it is not France that considers the "disarmament conference meaningless." Doumergue strongly stated that if France sits back and watches Germany's rearmament without taking precautions, France will be too late to regret it when a strong neighbor has grown its wings. Therefore, the government advocates that the discussion of the national defense expenditure case should not be delayed. Moreover, Germany has recently increased military spending and expanded its armaments. Doumergue concluded that if the national defense expenditure case is extended, he will take responsible actions based on his obligations. The audience applauded enthusiastically, except for the far left. (Havas News Agency, 14th)

Japanese Navy to Hold Large-Scale Exercises This Summer

(Tokyo) The Japanese Navy has decided to hold large-scale naval exercises in the seas off Kyushu, Korea, and Taiwan from the beginning of August. The Navy announced its plan on the 15th as follows: (1) Exercise period: from the beginning of August to the end of October, a total of three months (2) Exercise area: the seas near Honshu, Kyushu, Shikoku, Korea, and Taiwan (3) Participating troops: the First Fleet, the Second Fleet, and part of the Third Fleet, the Fourth Fleet (temporarily formed), Yokosuka, Wu, Sasebo, all garrison headquarters, Zhenhai, and Mako, a total of 80 warships and 200+ aircraft. (5) The purpose of the exercise is to test ship weapons, train soldiers, and enrich the Japanese Navy's strength on the front line of national defense. (Japan Union News, 15th)

(Tokyo) Navy Vice Officer Iwamura issued a statement saying that this year's naval exercise will be held during the hot summer and typhoon season, and will be supervised by Admiral Fushimi-no-miya. Foreign navies have all their warships participating in exercises, but due to budget constraints in the Japanese Navy, half of the warships stay in naval ports. Only the annual large-scale exercise can make up for this shortcoming. (Japan Union News, 15th)

(Nanjing) The authorities officially announced today that a large-scale naval exercise will be held around Japan's mainland and the seas around Kyushu, Korea, and Taiwan, starting in August and ending in October, supervised by Navy Chief of Staff Fushimi-no-miya, with a total of 180 large and small warships and more than 200 aircraft participating in the exercise. Airfield in the Middle of the Atlantic Ocean Begins to Be Used, Located on Noranha Island

(Paris) The first airfield in the middle of the Atlantic Ocean, located on Noranha Island, began to be used today. The famous French aviator Mermoz's large plane, the Rainbow, flew from Natal, Brazil, today to refuel there. The island is 125 miles from the eastern end of Brazil, one mile wide, and about five miles long. It has little to do with world commerce. Although many ships see it, few visit it. The island is located in the middle of the Atlantic Ocean and is a volcanic rock with trees and good scenery. There is a small farm on the top of the island. It was first discovered by Captain Noranha in 1503, so it is named after him. (Reuters, 14th)

German Propaganda Minister Visits Pilsudski, Places a Wreath at the Tomb of the Unknown Soldier: Polish Newspapers' Suspicion of Germany Is Difficult to Eradicate

Warsaw. German Propaganda Minister Goebbels arrived here yesterday. Today, General Pilsudski received him in a private capacity. Goebbels then went to the Tomb of the Unknown Soldier in Poland to place a wreath in front of the tomb to pay his respects. He registered his name in the guest book. It is heard that Goebbels is afraid that someone will plot against him, so news about his itinerary is not accurate in order to avoid accidents and ensure safety. Today, military police were densely stationed near the German embassy and on the main roads in the capital, and security was tight. When Goebbels paid tribute to the Tomb of the Unknown Soldier, idle people were driven away from the square in front of the tomb, and a large team of police stood around to protect him. All newspapers remained silent about Goebbels' visit and did not make any comments. (Note: Germany's demands on Poland are the return of the Corridor and the provinces of Posen and Upper Silesia.) International Labor Conference: Japanese Representative Defends Dumping Policy; General Assembly Passes 40-Hour Workweek Draft

(Geneva) Today, when the International Labor Bureau met in Geneva, Japanese government representative Yoshisaka spoke to defend Japan and refuted the accusations of social dumping. This morning's meeting continued to discuss the Labor Bureau's Director's report. The Japanese representative claimed that Japanese trade in 1929 and the years before the economic decline was greater than it is now, but no one has paid attention to this. Japan is working hard to restore prosperity, but to this day, all the results are not enough to absorb a small part of the unemployed. The Labor Bureau Director's report compares 1931 with 1933, which is actually inappropriate, because 1931 was an unusual year. He believes that 1929 should be used as the standard. According to 1933, Japanese world trade only accounted for 3.19% of world trade. Japanese export trade only accounted for 3.13% of world exports. Japan's imports are more than exports. Japan buys many raw materials and manufactured goods from foreign countries, which greatly helps the recovery of world trade. If Japan is forced to reduce its purchases of foreign goods, the world will suffer a major disadvantage. Japan did not use manpower to control currency. The depreciation of the Japanese yen was natural. If it is not allowed to depreciate, it will be manpower control. Finally, the Japanese representative thanked the International Labor Bureau for publishing the facts about Japan's industrial situation, and said that Japan's industrial situation is not worse than that of some European countries. (Reuters, 15th)

(Geneva) The International Labor Bureau Committee passed the draft of a 40-hour workweek today by 50 votes to 8. Employer representatives did not attend. (Reuters, 15th)

British House of Commons Questions Reform of the Shanghai Special Court: Eden Says He Has Obtained Sufficient Information; The Government Will Not Issue Any New Instructions for the Time Being

Germany Announces Suspension of Debt Payments: Creditor Countries Discuss Countermeasures; Bank for International Settlements Protests

(London) The creditor countries regard the German National Bank's announcement of suspending the payment of various debts for six months as an arbitrary act and are greatly panicked. The most relevant countries, such as Britain, France, the United States, the Netherlands, and Switzerland, are now discussing retaliatory measures. The British government stated at the beginning of debt negotiations that if Germany does not pay the Dawes and Young loans, the British government will take it seriously. What kind of actions the British government will take now has not yet been decided, but according to non-official predictions, the British government will adopt a kind of compulsory clearing house method. All Dawes and Young loans owed to Germany will be deducted from the German goods paid by Britain. Chancellor of the Exchequer Chamberlain agreed to make a statement on this matter in the House of Commons today. According to news from New York, the international banking community believes that if this suspension method is not revised, it will cause intense international disputes. After the National Bank announced the suspension of payments, the market price of German bonds fell. The Bank for International Settlements, the manager of the Young loan, held an emergency meeting and drafted a protest to be sent to the German government, opposing the suspension of interest payments on the Dawes and Young loans. It is heard that this protest leaves room for negotiation. According to today's news, the suspension of interest payments is a legal act of violating the Hague and Lausanne treaties. (Reuters, 15th)

Basel. The Bank for International Settlements will represent bondholders and reserve all the rights and interests of all bondholders, and will file a formal protest with the Berlin government, opposing the suspension of debt payments. The Bank for International Settlements' protest will announce that the suspension of debt payments violates the contracts under the Dawes and Young plans. (National Telegram, 15th)

(New York) The financial community today hopes that Germany will find a way to continue paying the reparations under the Dawes and Young plans. Since the announcement of the suspension of payments, German bonds have become stronger, because although foreign exchange cannot be paid for debt temporarily, it will still be paid in marks. It is generally believed here that Germany is prepared to negotiate with various countries in order to find a solution for continuing debt payments. The New York market was not affected by Germany's suspension announcement, because it was expected here. (National Telegram, 14th)

(Paris) Today, well-informed sources predict that the French government will levy special taxes on various payments to Germany to benefit the French who hold Dawes and Young bonds. (Reuters, 15th)

(New York) Today, the New York Times' Washington dispatch stated that if other governments file a formal protest against Germany's decision to suspend debt payments, the United States may also join the protest. (Reuters, 15th)

Italy and Four Other Countries Suspend Payment of War Debts to the United States

(Washington) Italy, Poland, Romania, and Hungary today jointly notified the United States that they would suspend payment of war debts due tomorrow. Therefore, the debtor country front has become unified. France and Belgium have already sent payment suspension notifications to the United States. Italy owes the United States a total of US$2,407,677,000. There had never been any delays in payments before 1932. Italy has repaid US$98,839,859 in war debts. From 1933, it adopted the British method of only making credit payments in order to avoid the name of delays in payments. However, the Johnson Act passed by the US Congress has included this credit payment in the list of delays in payments. Poland owes a total of US$435,687,550 in principal and interest. By the end of 1932, Poland had paid a total of US$3,302,980 and has not paid a penny since then. Romania's total debt is US$122,506,260, of which US$4,761,945 has been paid. Hungary owes a total of US$4,693,240 and had paid US$478,466 by the time payments were suspended in 1932. (National Telegram, 14th)

Exchange Rates

British-American: There was not much trading in the London foreign exchange market today. The opening exchange rate between British and American currencies was 5.05 yuan, the same as yesterday's closing exchange rate for the US dollar. Later, there were slight fluctuations. At 3 pm, it was 5.050625 yuan, an increase of 0625 yuan from the opening. Also, one US dollar is equivalent to three shillings and eleven pence 529 British gold.

British-French: The opening price was 76 francs 40, the same as yesterday's closing price. Later, it gradually rose to 76 francs 521. This is the most recent price.

American-British: The opening exchange rate for American and British currencies was 5.05125 yuan, an increase of 125 from yesterday's closing price. It then immediately fell to 500 yuan 05 cents, and there were no changes afterward.

American-French: The opening exchange rate for American and French currencies was 6.60 and a half, down by one-half from yesterday.

Cotton and Wheat

American Cotton: The cotton market first fell and then rose slightly. The Liverpool telegram was poor. The situation in Germany was uncertain, and the cotton belt weather was good, so the price fell. Then, colleagues purchased, and there was a risk of tropical storms, so the price rebounded slightly. Brokers advocated buying when the price fell.

Indian Cotton: In the Bombay cotton market, speculators sold off initially, and many parties closed out. Then, Japanese merchants bought in. The price of white Broch cotton for July and August delivery was 205 rupees 75, a decrease of 7 rupees.

British Cotton: The Liverpool cotton market was loose today. The price for July delivery was 6.34, lower than yesterday's closing by eight pounds.

British Wheat: The price of wheat in the Liverpool market for July delivery rose by 625 to 4 shillings and 8 pence.

Rubber

The London rubber market was sluggish. At noon, the transaction price for July and September delivery was 6 pence 5625, down 0625 from yesterday's closing.

The New York rubber market was quiet and slightly loose. Morale was good, but it was contained by labor strikes.

Securities

The opening prices of New York securities fluctuated slightly. The market was mixed. Merchants, in view of external news and developments, did not dare to buy or sell much. What is currently attracting the most attention is the steel industry dispute and the results of today's meeting to vote on a strike. Sun Ke Dined with Fu Zuoyi Yesterday

(Nanjing) Sun Ke hosted a lunch banquet for Fu Zuoyi on the 15th, and Lu Chao hosted a dinner banquet in the evening. (Central News Agency dispatch on the 15th)

National General Budget for the 23rd Year Compiled

(Nanjing) The national general budget for the 23rd year was compiled by the Directorate General of Budget, Accounting and Statistics on the 14th and submitted to the National Government. It was sent to the Central Political Council for discussion on the 15th. The budget includes the following: miscellaneous tax revenue of more than 36 million yuan, accounting for 46 percent; salt tax of more than 10 million yuan, accounting for 24 percent; consolidated tax of more than 11 million yuan, accounting for 15 percent; tobacco and alcohol tax of more than 2.3 million yuan, accounting for 3 percent; stamp tax of more than 1.2 million yuan, accounting for 1 percent; state-owned enterprise income accounting for 3 percent; administrative income and aid revenue accounting for 1 percent each; the rest are all less than 1 percent. Military expenditure accounts for 39 percent, the figures are verified and have been reduced compared with previous years. Debt service fees account for more than 25 million yuan, accounting for 34 percent, but this includes more than 10 million yuan for repaying debt principal and more than 3.8 million yuan for paying Boxer indemnity principal and interest. Financial expenditure accounts for 9 percent, education and cultural expenditure accounts for 3 percent, subsidies account for 6 percent, foreign affairs, construction and internal affairs each account for more than 1 percent, while transportation, industry, party affairs, pensions, justice, and Mongolian and Tibetan affairs each account for less than 1 percent. (Central News Agency dispatch on the 15th)

Closing of the People's Movement Work Discussion Conference

(Nanjing) The National People's Movement Work Discussion Conference held its fifth meeting at 8:00 am on the 15th. 50 people attended. Ma Chaojun chaired the meeting. Chen Gongbo reported on his experiences and thoughts from his inspection of Southeast Asia. More than 20 proposals were then passed. Jiang Qingyun, Chen Shiquan, and Xu Wentian were elected to draft an open letter to the public. The meeting adjourned. The sixth meeting was held at 2:00 pm. Wang Qi chaired the meeting and reported on the central people's movement's implementation outline for future work. The open letter to the public was passed. The closing ceremony was held at 4:00 pm. After Wang's speech, Sun Ke gave instructions and put forward three major goals for future work: (1) Autonomy, (2) Self-defense, and (3) Self-sufficiency. Representatives from various regions were scheduled to leave Beijing on the 16th. (Central News Agency dispatch on the 15th)

Three Ministries Discuss the Establishment of a Maritime Court

(Nanjing) The Executive Yuan has instructed the Ministries of Transportation, Navy, and Judicial Administration to jointly draft a proposal for the establishment of a maritime court submitted by the Ministry of Transportation, and submit it to the Yuan for approval. Now, the Ministry of Transportation has received repeated requests from shipping guilds in various cities to promptly establish a maritime arbitration organization due to frequent ship collisions recently. In the recent case of the Jing'an ship of the Sanbei Shipping Company, the case was detained by the Shanghai Local Court. The Shanghai Shipping Industry Association telegraphed the ministry again, requesting that before a maritime arbitration organization is established, a temporary arbitration office should be established first to specifically hear the case. According to the telegram, the Ministry of Transportation believes that it is not appropriate to establish a temporary arbitration office before a maritime arbitration organization is established, and has instructed the association to be informed. However, it intends to promote the early establishment of a maritime arbitration organization to meet the needs and has consulted the Ministry of Judicial Administration, requesting that a meeting be scheduled for consultations to proceed, so that it can be submitted to the Yuan for approval and established as soon as possible. (Special dispatch on the 15th)

Ministry of Finance Consults with Various Provinces Again to Investigate and Prohibit Private Cigarette Production in Various Counties

(Nanjing) The Ministry of Finance consulted with various provinces again, ordering the public security bureaus of various counties to earnestly investigate and prohibit the private production of cigarettes, and if any are seized, to jointly punish them in accordance with the law together with the consolidated tax authorities, and to handle them strictly in accordance with the law. British Trade War Against Japan (London Correspondence) Cannot Tolerate the Oppression of Japanese Goods Anymore; Must Immediately Fix the British Market

The economic opposition between the United Kingdom and Japan has recently become increasingly serious. The United Kingdom must maintain its vested interests, especially its economic superiority in its autonomous colonies. However, Japan is unwilling to easily concede and withdraw from the sphere of influence of the United Kingdom. Moreover, after withdrawing, there is no suitable alternative location. Therefore, in order to coordinate this trade opposition relationship, representatives selected by the private sector held meetings locally, but ultimately broke down because they could not agree on the export volume and market division. Since that meeting broke down, Japan has further promoted its exports to the United Kingdom, while the United Kingdom has only engaged in defense. Another matter of great concern to the United Kingdom is that although the United Kingdom is an advanced country in imperialism, the spinning industry still occupies a very important position in the industry. However, from 1931 to 1933, during these three years, the number of spinning spindles in the United Kingdom decreased by 6,981,000 spindles. On the contrary, in Japan, it increased by 1,450,000 spindles. In comparison, how angry is the United Kingdom? Therefore, Secretary of Commerce Runciman issued a statement, the gist of which is as follows:

"The British government has drawn the attention of the Japanese government to the problem of competition from Japanese goods for two years now. During this period, the export of Japanese goods has continued to increase. Therefore, the British government has had no choice but to come to the conclusion of trade self-defense. However, it does not itself believe that the commercial relations treaty of the past twenty years needs to be broken. However, the government believes that the silk tariff issue cannot be delayed any longer. Therefore, the Finance Minister has ordered the Tariff Advisory Committee to complete its report as soon as possible, and requests the authorities of colonies and protectorates outside Africa to implement appropriate quota systems. This quota system is the quota for the import of cotton products and rayon products from foreign countries. The number should be based on the average import volume from 1927 to 1931. The colonial governments should immediately formulate this necessary law. It is expected that the law requires that imports not hinder the implementation of the quota system and can take effect immediately (May 7). The West African colonies have already notified the cancellation of the Anglo-Japanese treaty on May 16 of last year because the treaty hinders the preferences for British products. In the future, methods will be sought to restrict Japanese products. I am issuing this statement because I do not want to involve issues other than cotton products and rayon products, and the government believes that competition with Japan should not be limited to cotton products and rayon products. Therefore, it is considering what kind of tariff policy should be implemented on other commodities in the colonial market. As for the United Kingdom itself, the government considers the above-mentioned tariff law as a general countermeasure. No matter what proposals Japan puts forward on this issue, if a mutually agreed solution is proposed, (the United Kingdom) is certainly willing to give it deep consideration and attention."

This statement is no different from a commercial "ultimatum" to Japan. The United Kingdom still firmly insists that the average number of Japanese exports from 1928 to 1931 should be the base. Let us briefly examine the figures for these five years. The average Japanese cotton cloth exports to India in these four years was 436.869 thousand square yards, cotton cloth exports to the Straits Settlements were 32.818 thousand square yards, cotton cloth exports to Egypt were 99.454 thousand square yards, and to Australia were 15.285 thousand square yards. By 1933, India had increased to 451.803 thousand square yards, the Straits Settlements had increased to 95.769 thousand square yards, Egypt had increased to 21.351 thousand square yards, and Australia had increased to 54.997 thousand square yards. Other British territories, except Hong Kong, were mostly monopolized by Japanese cotton products. The United Kingdom, as the ruler, has retreated to a passive position. At this time, of course, it must try to counterattack as soon as possible. In terms of various autonomous colonies, there is indeed no clear expression of attitude at present, but Australia still harbors fear of Japan, Canada is even more heavily guarded, and India and Egypt are better to Japan only if there are exchange conditions (for example, requiring Japan to purchase Indian cotton). Most of the rest are transferred by the will of the United Kingdom itself. In short, the degree of opposition in the economic relationship between the United Kingdom and Japan is becoming increasingly profound. (May 9)

Japanese Puppets Drafting Soldiers in the Northeast; Different Numbers Drafted from Each Village; Villagers' Cries Shake the Heavens

Tianjin Correspondence: A person from Shenyang said that the Japanese recently ordered the puppet State Military and Political Department to implement conscription, starting from the southern part of the puppet Fengtian Province, divided into three types of villages: A, B, and C, to determine the number of draftees. Villages of type A with more than 100 households will draft 80 people, about one person from each household; villages of type B with more than 50 households will send one person per household, about 40 people; villages of type C with more than 20 households will draft 20 people, one person from each household. After conscription, they will be trained by Japanese instructors in the puppet garrison command headquarters in various places. It is said that this type of recruitment is in preparation for defense against Russia. Liaoyang, Liaozhong, Shenyang, and Xinmin counties have already started recruitment. A few days ago, 80 young men were drafted from Nanshuchihutun, Shenyang. Villagers, men, women, old and young, cried and wailed, seeing them off for more than ten miles and unwilling to part. The misery is indescribable. Rumors of a war between Japan and Russia have been spreading even more intensely recently. A branch of the volunteer army of two or three thousand people has also been found in the Andong area, elusive and moving unpredictably along the Anfeng Railway line, making it impossible for the Japanese army to grasp its whereabouts. According to the Japanese investigation, this volunteer army is determined to be led by Yang Yaojun, the former department of Li Du and Ding Chao. They were defeated in the Chulin Mishan last year and retreated to Russian territory. After being trained by the Soviet Union, they were ordered to return to the eastern region to serve as a separate detachment when a war between Japan and Russia occurs in the future. Therefore, the Japanese army is deeply afraid that this volunteer army will expand its power and disrupt the rear, and has sent aircraft to search for its headquarters everywhere. In Shenyang City, large and small businesses have been extremely desolate for half a year, and all merchants have no business to speak of. For example, Ruilinxiang shop in Brick City only sells two to three hundred yuan per day, less than one-fifth of what it was before the incident. The city is heavily guarded. Every day after 8 or 9 pm, the police hold large guns and set up posts on the main thoroughfares, inspecting passersby. After 10 pm, even with a pass or as a member of an organization, it is difficult to pass. The Japanese oppression of the people in southern Fengtian is increasing day by day. Tangmazhai, west of Liaoyang and Anshan, is the confluence of the Hunhe River and the Taizi River. There are more than ten agricultural villages clustered on both banks. Because the Taizi River floods every summer and autumn, the farmland on both banks is always destroyed by thousands of acres. Therefore, more than ten villages raised funds to build two dikes for flood prevention, which have been repaired by the villages over the years. On the 7th of this month, some Japanese and Koreans rented hundreds of acres of rice fields on the west bank of the river and established a rice field company, wanting to dig up the dikes and divert water for irrigation. The farmers in dozens of villages, because their lives and properties are at stake, came forward to stop them. The Japanese refused to listen and continued to dig. The villagers were furious and gathered more than 4,000 people to protect the dikes, living on the dikes day and night, with food and drink delivered by women. The Japanese and Koreans ran to the Japanese army in Liaoyang, saying that the villagers were anti-Manchu. A large team was dispatched and opened fire on the farmers in several rows, killing dozens of people. The villagers remained united and did not disperse. The Japanese army had no choice but to capture several people, designated them as representatives, and ordered everyone to disperse, but the villagers did not give in. The stalemate has lasted for five or six days, and no results have yet been obtained. (12th)

Sixth Route Army Captures Biaohu; Remnants Flee from Yuexi, Retreating to Xingguo

Nanchang Dispatch: The Sixth Route Army, under Xue Yue, tasked with advancing from Yongfeng towards Xingguo and Ningdu, forming a pincer movement with the Third Route Army advancing from Guangchang. After recovering Longgang, Xue's troops immediately began building a road from Yongfeng through Longgang to Xingguo territory. At that time, the fake 23rd Division of Sun Chaoqun, the fake Western Independent Regiment 123, and various local guerrillas, constructed pillboxes and strong fortifications at Biaohu (south of Longgang) to prevent the National Army from advancing. Commander-in-Chief Xue, in order to complete the road from Longgang to Gulonggang, and to destroy the pillboxes and blockade the bandit areas, ordered Han Hanying's troops to attack south. On the 3rd of this month, at Xiazhang, fifteen miles south of Longgang, they discovered bandit fortresses built by the fake 23rd Division on the high mountains of Biaohu on the west bank of the river. Zhang's regiment of Han's division immediately forced a crossing and launched a frontal attack on the bandits. Tan Desheng, the fake commander of the 67th Regiment, and Yu Chujie, the commander of the 69th Regiment, personally supervised the battle at the front line. The National Army fought bravely, pressing forward step by step. After three hours of fighting, they completely captured Biaohu. The remaining bandits retreated from Yuexi and Liangcun into Xingguo territory. Xingguo is only a few dozen miles from Gulonggang, with mountains upon mountains, and was once the lair of the Red Bandits. Further advance must wait until the roads are repaired, and the rear supply and deployment are complete. However, judging from the current situation, it is expected that by the end of this year, the various route armies will be able to completely recover Xingguo, Yudu, Huichang, Ruijin, Ningdu, and Shicheng. (13th)

Southeast and East Route Armies Encircle Western Fujian Bandit Area; Longyan to Xinquan Highway Completed

Shantou Dispatch: Jiang Bocheng arrived in Guangdong on the 7th and consulted with Commanders-in-Chief Chen and Li regarding bandit suppression plans. The First and Second Columns of Guangdong will attack Huichang and Yudu within a short time. At the same time, the troops of Huang Renhuan and Chen Zhang stationed in Yongding, Shanghang, and Wuping in western Fujian, together with the East Route Army, will encircle Changting. According to military news today, the Red Bandits in northern Fujian are currently gathered in Changting, Ruijin, Shicheng, Gucheng, Ninghua, Qingxi, and Guihua, numbering about 40,000 to 50,000, but their combat power is extremely weak. The highway from Longyan to Xinquan was completed last month through the cooperation of the military and civilians. Last month, the Central Army advanced to Baisha, and from Baisha, Hexi, Chadi, and Taiba, advanced to Jiuxian in Shanghang. Everywhere they went, the Communist bandits scattered at the mere sight of them. Now, they have moved from northern Fujian to western Fujian. The National Army encircling the bandit area has very strong forces. Last month, when the Central Army advanced to attack Guangchang, they fought fiercely with the bandits for four days and nights, and the main force of the Red Bandits was almost completely annihilated. The bandits in Fujian and Jiangxi now are large in number but lack quality, merely having an empty appearance. After the Central Army advanced into Liancheng, Zhong Zhaokui's troops moved from Lanjia Ferry and stationed in Baisha. Another unit patrols back and forth in the area bordering Yongding and Shanghang. A few days ago, more than a thousand Communist bandits raided Dajing but were defeated by Zhong's troops. More than thirty female Communist bandits were captured alive, all of whom were young women. More than two hundred female bandits are also imprisoned in Shanghang Prison, all of whom were captured on the front lines. Luo Pai, near Changting, has the fake army's Independent 8th Regiment, with 500 to 600 rifles, specializing in disturbing Bingguofang on the Fujian-Guangdong border. Lian Rihui has joined forces with the local militia to search and suppress them, and they have retreated to the rear. (8th)

Former Henan Industry Department Head, Zhu Tingfen, Commits Suicide in Poverty in Jinan; Appointment Arrives Hours After Death; Well-wishers Unaware, Mourners at the Door

Jinan Dispatch: Zhu Tingfen was a native of Gushi County, Henan, over fifty years old. It is said that he graduated from the Army University in Beiping during the late Qing Dynasty and even served as the school's principal. After the Republic, when Wu Ziyu stationed troops in Henan, Zhu served as the head of the Henan Industry Department and concurrently as the Land Reclamation Director. He was upright and honest, leaving office with no savings. His circumstances have worsened in recent years. Because he had a fellow-township relationship with Zhang Honglie, the head of the Shandong Construction Department, he traveled to Jinan this spring, seeking a place to settle. Zhang, noting that there was work here but there were more monks than porridge, said it would be difficult to arrange something immediately, providing some funds and asking him to wait. Zhu stayed at the Tianxiang Inn in Xian Dong Xiang in the city from March 7th, feeling depressed and bored. For months, he had not found a place to eat. Recently, Zhang Honglie recommended Zhu to the Salt Affairs Audit Office. Yesterday, he completed the appointment, appointing Zhu as a counselor and supervisor of the Qingdao Salt Fields, with a monthly salary of over one hundred yuan. That evening, it was sent to Zhang's place. Today (the 13th) at eight o'clock, Zhu Tingfen got up as usual and went to a nearby Douzhi shop for breakfast, then returned to the inn (Room 4 downstairs). Afterwards, he was not seen leaving. Zhang Honglie sent someone to deliver the appointment to Zhu at eight in the morning. The inn's tea servant saw that the room door was unlocked and there was no one inside, and replied that Zhu had gone out and would return shortly. From morning to afternoon, the messenger went several times but did not see him. It was not until four o'clock in the afternoon that the female owner of the inn went upstairs to look for something (there were no other guests upstairs) and discovered that Zhu had hanged himself. He had been dead for some time. The inn reported it to the Construction Department. Zhang Honglie, noting that Zhu had been in Jinan for several months and had only secured work today, yet Zhu died on this very day, a difference of only a few hours, lamented his tragic fate. He notified his family (Zhu has an old wife and five sons) on the one hand, and sent someone to report to the court for an inspection, buying a coffin for the burial. Fellow Henan townsmen in Jinan heard the news and went to offer condolences, all sighing deeply.

It is said that Zhu was most proficient in mathematics. Recently, he had a work sent to the Commercial Press for publication. Although he was depressed in the inn, he showed no other signs before his death. However, a week ago, he said to someone, "My mathematical skills are unmatched. I have gained insights from studying integrals, and I have made a final work. I am afraid I will die soon." At the time, the listener thought it was a joke, but unexpectedly, Zhu hanged himself. How tragic! (13th)

Qingpu: Fire at Kerosene Depot Injures Person

Shen Zhongqing, a kerosene merchant in this county, opened a Yuanmao kerosene depot in his own residence on Dongmen Street. Since starting the business, his situation has been good. However, in late April of this year, he suffered a fire, and his son was burned, and has not yet recovered. After this setback, the merchant, in order to maintain his livelihood, tried to raise funds and obtain loans to rebuild a new house on the original site for both residential and business use. At the same time, he opened a branch store in Fangjia Yao in District 12 to start business first. Unexpectedly, less than two months later, the branch store suffered another fire at noon the day before yesterday. In an instant, all the houses and goods were reduced to ashes, and a clerk in the store was burned. It is said that the injury is quite serious and his life is in danger.

Suzhou: New Police Chief Takes Office

Shen Wei, the police chief of Wu County, was ordered to be transferred to the police chief of Changshu County. Wang Bolin was appointed to fill the vacancy. Wang was appointed and came to Suzhou, originally scheduled to take office on the 14th. Because the predecessor did not complete the handover procedures, it was changed to yesterday (the 15th) at 9:00 am to take office.

Chefang Township Robbery Injures Person

On the night of the 14th, two bandit boats carrying more than ten bandits arrived at Chenjia Ham in Chefang Township. After landing, they first swarmed into the home of villager Wu Yiwu to rob. They beat and injured his nephew Wu Yujiang. They then went to the homes of Chen Junxian and Zhang Linzhao to search and rob, and then fled with their loot. It is estimated that the three families lost about five or six hundred yuan.

Wuxi: Anti-Smoking Conference Resolves Important Cases

The Wuxi County Anti-Smoking Personnel Conference has hired Li Tiping, Qian Sunqing, and Gu Shuzhi as committee members, appointed by Concurrent Chairman Yan and local officials. Later, Gu Shuzhi firmly requested to resign, and Cheng Jingtang was hired as a committee member instead. Yao Fusheng was appointed as secretary, Hua Hongtao as the general affairs section chief, Chen Yuchu concurrently as the investigation section chief, Zhu Yuancheng as the license section chief, and Jiang Zhizhen as the audit section chief, to handle various affairs and report to the Provincial Anti-Smoking Committee for approval. Yesterday, the first committee meeting was held, and the following matters were resolved: (1) Designating Puren, Tongren, and the Sanatorium, and the Physicians Association to handle the smoking cessation center and scheduling regular meetings to coordinate methods. (2) Future regular meetings will be held twice a month, and temporary meetings will be held as needed. At this point, the registration and licensing procedures for smokers have been actively prepared. Officially designated native opium dens: two native opium dens are allowed to be set up in the Wuxi urban area, divided into four grades: A, B, C, and D. Those who hold licenses will pay donations according to the grade. Grade A will pay 2,400 yuan per year, Grade B will pay 1,400 yuan, Grade C will pay 800 yuan, and Grade D will pay 400 yuan. Once the number of native opium dens and opium shops is limited by the County Anti-Smoking Committee, no new ones will be allowed to be added, and they will be gradually reduced each year, completely banned within four years. As for opium sales points, they are not currently being established for the sake of caution. The total number of smokers has never been statistically counted. Now, according to the provincial order to urgently investigate and report the exact number of smokers, based on the confirmed number of smokers who obtained licenses during the anti-smoking campaign in 1918, estimated to be more than 15,000 people, it was decided to report first in order to obtain licenses.

Silk Factories Continue to Request Exemption from Improvement Fees

Xinyi, Xingji, Yuji, and eighteen other silk factories are against the Silkworm Model Area's collection of three yuan per load of dry cocoons for improvement fees. Because the dry cocoons transported by each factory to the city have been detained, the raw material supply has been cut off, and the factories are about to stop production. The livelihoods of most female workers are in danger. Yesterday, they continued to meet and resolved as follows: (1) Continue to submit a petition to the Model Area to fight for exemption and ask the Chamber of Commerce to request the release of the detained cocoon ships first. (2) Telegraph to fellow businesses in various counties in this area to fight for exemption together. (3) Recently, some people claiming to be inspectors freely enter the factories without any courtesy, hindering work, and should be unanimously rejected and not allowed to enter the factory. The county government believes that the improvement fees collected by the Model Area are used for improving the silkworm industry, which is of great interest to the silk merchants themselves. The factories' firm opposition is unreasonable. In addition to issuing an order not to allow it, it also intends to summon representatives of each factory, Chen Geshu and others, to the government to talk and persuade them. The Chamber of Commerce is also deeply concerned about various extreme measures and has invited Qian Fenghao and Hua Shaochun, the chairmen of the silk factory and cocoon industry guilds, to the meeting to coordinate and find a proper solution.

Liu Zhuomin Sentenced to Imprisonment

Liu Zhuomin, the former chief of the Second Public Security Branch, was found guilty of obstructing official duties for resisting the handover. His wife, Wen Rongzhen, was found guilty of insulting public officials on the spot. The local branch court interrogated and detained them, which also led to the mutual accusations between Gu Renfa and Li Shuyun. The details have been reported in this newspaper. It is now learned that Liu Zhuomin and his wife, after being prosecuted by the prosecutor, were tried by Judge Liu Bingzhen of the criminal court, and the verdict was announced yesterday (the 15th) at 10:00 am. Liu Zhuomin was sentenced to six months of imprisonment for concealing items under his official control as a public official. Liu Wen was sentenced to forty-five days of detention for insulting public officials on the spot while they were performing their duties according to law. After the verdict, Liu Zhuomin was returned to detention, while Wen Rongzhen was released on bail with a written guarantee of five hundred yuan.

Kidnappers Riot in Prison

Zhu Yunting, a famous doctor in the northern suburbs of this county, was previously kidnapped twice by bandits and was finally released after paying a ransom of one thousand yuan. Later, Qian Tianxiong, the captain of the county water patrol, arrested Yu Hailin, a key criminal in the case, in Shanghai and brought him back to the county for interrogation and detention. Unexpectedly, Yu, incorrigibly wicked, behaved lawlessly in prison, bullying fellow prisoners. Yesterday, during mealtime, after the prisoners finished their silk reeling work in the workshop, they were about to eat when Yu suddenly had a quarrel with a prisoner over a minor matter and then started fighting. The prisoner was severely beaten with an iron tool, causing injuries all over his body and unable to move. Seeing this, the other prisoners became indignant and questioned Yu. Yu shouted loudly, "I am a kidnapper, a more serious crime. My treatment is different from yours. You must give me some consideration in everything!" His attitude was arrogant and unreasonable. Then, a prison worker reported the situation to Warden Xing Yuantang, who led armed police to suppress the riot, and they dispersed. Afterwards, the prisoners, in the name of the entire group, made two requests to the authorities: (1) Yu Hailin is lawless in prison and should be punished severely, with the death penalty. (2) Or transfer the prisoner to the judiciary for handling.

Yangzhou: Ministry of Finance Abolishes Deputy Transport Commissioner's Office

Zhou Zonghua, the manager of the Yangzhou Salt Affairs Audit Branch and concurrently the Deputy Transport Commissioner of Lianghuai, after being ordered to be transferred to the Zhejiang Hangzhou Audit Branch and concurrently the Salt Transport Commissioner of Lianghuai, his vacancy has been filled by Yao Jingyu. Now it is heard that the Salt Affairs Department of the Ministry of Finance, feeling that the auditing affairs in the southern Huai area are becoming more leisurely and in order to economize public funds, plans to abolish the Gutang Branch and the Yangzhou Deputy Transport Commissioner's Office, and change Yangzhou to an Audit Branch subordinate to northern Huai. It is also heard that Niu Jianxia, who previously served as the assistant of the Gutang Branch, has been confirmed as the assistant of the Yangzhou Branch.

Changshu: Policeman Attempts Extortion, Frightens Woman to Death

Shen Zhenxing, who privately set up a smoking den in Machao, Hanbeimen Street, had a mistress, Zhang, who ran the business at home. Unexpectedly, on the evening of the 13th, three men dressed in long robes and wearing yellow police trousers, resembling policemen, entered the Shen family's house intending to extort money. The woman, seeing their fierce appearance, ran out wildly and suddenly fell to the ground outside the house, dying. The three men, realizing that they had caused trouble, fled together. Afterwards, the family tried to save her and urgently called a Western doctor to examine her, but it was too late to revive her. Her family felt resentful because the policemen had extorted and threatened her to death, and requested the authorities to investigate and bring the policemen to justice.

Famous Library Almost Destroyed by Fire

The Tieqin Tongjianlou Library, a famous Chinese library belonging to the Qu family, was built in Jinlilu Village outside the east gate of this county. However, the valuable books inside have all been moved to Shanghai. Now, the site contains only an ancient building and ordinary books. The day before yesterday afternoon, a fire suddenly broke out at the Qu family's house. Because the countryside lacks firefighting equipment, it soon became a raging fire. Although there were many villagers, they had no way to extinguish it. The Tieqin Tongjianlou Library was nearby, in great danger, and everyone was alarmed. They urgently used the telephone to hire a gasoline boat from the city fire department to rush to the rescue, and fortunately, it was extinguished immediately. The library was unharmed, but many houses belonging to the Qu Wenqing family and the nearby Zhu family's hotel were destroyed, resulting in significant losses.

Hangzhou: Hangzhou Republic Daily Reorganized into Southeast Daily

Since the Hangzhou Republic Daily purchased a web printing press last year, increased its pages, reformed its layout, and enriched its content, its sales volume has increased sharply from 12,000 to over 20,000 copies within nine months. Its distribution area has expanded to various provinces in the southeast. As highways in various provinces are gradually being built, Hangzhou is gradually becoming the transportation center of seven provinces: Jiangsu, Zhejiang, Anhui, Fujian, Hunan, Jiangxi, and Hubei. The Oriental Grand Port is also being actively surveyed. The newspaper's president, Hu Jianzhong, consulted with the editor-in-chief, Liu Xiangnu, and decided to further implement a major reform plan. He requested the Provincial Party Department to allow the newspaper to be jointly run by public and private interests, to solicit new shares and form a board of directors. Zhang Daofan, Chen Bulei, Chen Guofu, Ye Chucang, Chen Lifu, Guo Renyuan, Zheng Yi, Fang Qingxu, Luo Tian, Xu Shaodi, Zhang Qiang, Ye Suzhong, Hu Jianzhong, and other thirteen people will be directors, with Chen Guofu as chairman. Wang Tingyang, Xiao Zheng, Zheng Wenli, Hong Ludong, and Pan Gongzhan will be supervisors. The newspaper's name will be changed to Southeast Daily, expanding the pages to four large sheets, increasing various staff members, greatly expanding news coverage, and adding a Legal Commentary section and a Social Stock Affairs section. In addition to removing reading materials and sofas, Wu Zhaochun, Di Zhongwen, and others have been added. It is said that after the newspaper is renovated, branch offices will be set up in major cities.

Special Article

Impressions of Economic Survey of Guangxi Province (Continued)

— Qian Jiaju

Binyang is a handicraft area in Guangxi and is also the most famous place for producing porcelain. Because there are more people than land in this place, residents are engaged in a kind of handicraft to maintain their lives, and people are rich in imitation, so it is also known as "Little Japan". They can imitate all kinds of small toys, such as felt hats, copper and iron utensils, curtain hooks, children's toys, and even imitate Mauser pistols. Often there is a village where the residents of the entire village are engaged in a kind of handicraft, and this handicraft has become a special product of this village. For example, people in Fangcun weave wick cords, people in Shikan village make paper fans and paper quilts, people in Cucun make small iron utensils for daily use, Wang Xie village makes mud baskets and lamp ropes, people in Dazhuang village make rain hats, Mengcun make mats, Shicun make pestles, Shangzhai village make combs, Luocun make pens, Donglu Mengcun weave sleeves, Yangcun make hats, Donghai village make toothbrushes... They are engaged in this kind of work all year round. The things they make are carried to the market to sell. Binyang has a Lixu, which is one of the four largest markets in Guangxi, a market every three days. It is not only a distribution center for import and export goods in the county, but also a general meeting place for commodity trade in neighboring counties in Binyang. On the day of the market, these craftsmen, whether making hats, umbrellas, copper and iron utensils... stop work. They get up early and carry their burdens to Lixu. Lixu is a town ten miles away from the city. The excitement and tension of this day are extraordinary. It is really a sea of people, and the voices are boiling, just like the factory temple of the old lunar year in Beiping. It is not until four or five o'clock in the afternoon that people slowly disperse. After this market period, Lixu becomes like a dead city, with the shop doors ajar, business is bleak, like the atmosphere of the New Year when every family closes its doors in our mainland. Here, we can not only see that Guangxi's commerce is still staying in the market system, but also that craftsmen are also part-time traveling merchants. The organization of this kind of feudal economy is unexpected for those of us who are used to living in big cities.

Binyang porcelain is to Guangxi as Jingdezhen porcelain is to Jiangxi, although Jingde porcelain has a domestic market, Binyang porcelain has only a part of the provincial market. The discovery of Binyang porcelain is said to have a history of more than 80 years. It originated in Laoyao Village. At that time, only unglazed pottery was made. Later, people from Jiangxi served in the army in Yunnan and Guizhou. They passed through Binyang and their funds were cut off. They went to Laoyao Village to work. Within two or three years, they discovered white glaze stone and began to study how to apply a rough glaze. Later, Jiang of Lusi (village name) sent people to Jingdezhen, Liling and other places in Jiangxi to investigate the manufacturing method and study pigments. In recent years, with the promotion of the authorities, the manufacturing method has been greatly improved. In July of the year before last, the Construction Department specially hired technicians to investigate and test the porcelain quality in the area. As a result, they found that the clay quality here was inferior to Jiangxi but better than Shanghai. However, because the method used was too crude, 400 yuan was allocated to encourage them. Local kiln owners were also very enthusiastic at this time, raising a total of 2,000 yuan, and then borrowing 4,000 yuan from the Construction Department, and then established a new porcelain factory. Now the factory is managed by the Bureau of Industry and Commerce. The porcelain they produce is much better than the native method. This kind of porcelain is completely imitating Jiangxi porcelain and improving it. Although it is not as fine as the products of Jiangxi, it is completely different from the local porcelain. However, their products are not many now, and there are no sellers on the market. According to the Guangxi authorities, their purpose of improving Binyang porcelain is not to compete with Jiangxi porcelain or imported products in the market outside the province. They only hope that Binyang improved porcelain will be able to seize the position of Jiangxi porcelain and Guangdong porcelain in the provincial market in the future, because until now, Binyang native porcelain can only be sold to the remote counties in the upper reaches of the Xijiang River. From Guixian downstream, as well as Nanning, Liuzhou, Guilin, Yulin... The market is filled with Hunan porcelain and Jiangxi porcelain. Therefore, if Binyang porcelain is promoted, a part of the leak in Guangxi Province can also be resisted.

In addition to the new porcelain factory, Binyang probably has more than 300 kilns and more than 20 kilns. The total value of porcelain produced each year is about 150,000 to 160,000 yuan. They often use one kiln together, each kiln has nine sections, the first and last two sections are empty, and there are seven sections that can be filled with things, so each kiln has as few as seven or eight households and as many as thirteen or fourteen households. This kind of kiln is often the only production tool inherited from their ancestors.
