Local News

Today: Memorial Service for Premier Sun's Guangzhou Tragedy, 9:00 AM at the City Party Headquarters in Fenglinqiao; Strict Guard by Military Police Throughout the City

Today is the 12th anniversary of Premier Sun's Guangzhou Tragedy. Various circles in the city will hold a memorial service at the City Party Headquarters in Fenglinqiao at 9:00 AM. The City Party Headquarters will also issue a letter to the public. The entire city will fly flags at half-mast in commemoration. It is also heard that various military and police agencies, considering today as a revolutionary memorial and also the abolished lunar Dragon Boat Festival, are afraid that unscrupulous elements will take the opportunity to disrupt public order. Therefore, they have specially ordered their subordinate military police to strengthen their defenses and add double posts on important transportation routes to be prepared. All illegal parades and gatherings will be strictly prohibited.

General Manager of Sichuan Minsheng Company, Lu Zuofu, Arrives in Shanghai Yesterday; Talks Freely About the Recent Situation in Sichuan Province and the Company

Lu Zuofu, a Sichuan industrialist and general manager of Minsheng Industrial Company, arrived in Shanghai yesterday afternoon at 1:00 PM on the Minsheng Company's Yongnian Wheel from Chongqing. A reporter from the Xinsheng Society met with Lu at the Minsheng Shanghai Branch yesterday and heard him express the following:

Bandit Suppression Completed

Since Xu Xiangqian's unit, the fake Fourth Front Army of the Communist bandits in western Hubei, sneaked into Sichuan, Supervisor Liu Xiang has cooperated with various armies and divided into six routes to encircle and suppress them: First Route Deng Xihou, Second Route Tian Songyao, Third Route Li Jiayu, Fourth Route Yang Sen, Fifth Route Tang Shizun, Sixth Route Liu Bangjun. Initially, there were about 150,000 Communist bandits. After phased and painful suppression, they have gradually been eliminated. The Communist bandits are hiding in Tongjiang and Wanyuan counties, with about 40,000 to 50,000 bandits. The general attack order for the fourth phase of encirclement and suppression has been issued, and the number of suppression troops has been increased. It is expected that they can be completely eliminated within sixty days. At the same time, food to the bandit areas has been cut off, so the bandits are feeling a great shortage of food. Unless there are unexpected events, the bandit suppression plan will be completed as scheduled.

Construction Begins

Supervisor Liu Xiang recently held a production and construction conference in Chengdu. Various administrative officials and local gentry and merchants participated in the conference and decided on many construction methods, which have now begun and are being carried out separately. As for the highways in Sichuan Province, such as Chongqing, Chengdu, Tongchuan, Guang'an, and Shunqing, they have all been connected and long-distance buses are running, making transportation very convenient. After the bandit suppression is completed, they will engage in post-war reconstruction and reorganize the army to carry out construction work with full force.

Consolidation of Taxes and Currency

Various tax rules in Sichuan Province have now begun to be consolidated, based on the principle of a single tax system. The detailed methods are still under discussion, but the kerosene and cigarette tax rules have already implemented a single tax system. In short, everything will only be successful after the bandit suppression is completed. The lack of uniformity of currency is also being consolidated. The Sichuan Mint has stopped minting currency.

The Sichuan armies in Chengdu and Chongqing both commonly use Sun Premier's currency. However, it is not commonly used outside of Sichuan province because the silver content is slightly lower.

Company Business

Minsheng Industrial Company has (A) operating businesses, now divided into three categories: (1) Shipping, operating on the upper and lower reaches of the Yangtze River, with a total of twenty-eight ships, totaling approximately seven thousand tons. (2) Machine factory, located in Chongqing. (3) Power plant, located in Hechuan, which has been in operation for eight years. The initial capital was eight thousand yuan, with more than six hundred shareholders. The capital has been increased year by year, and now it has reached 1,169,500 yuan. Accumulated public reserve funds and insurance are about 1 million yuan, totaling approximately 2 million yuan. (B) Investment businesses: (1) Beichuan Railway, totaling 100,000 yuan, from Datiankan to Baimiaozi, 16 kilometers long, on the banks of the Jialing River. It is now planned to extend the railway to the Qu River, approximately 60 kilometers. This railway is a light-rail type, specializing in coal transportation. (3) Coal mines, totaling three locations, on the banks of the Jialing River and in Yunyang, totaling 50,000 yuan. The above two items are Minsheng Company's investments in local construction.

Social Enterprises

(1) The China Western Scientific Research Institute, located on the banks of the Jialing River, is divided into four departments: Biology, Agriculture and Forestry, Geology, and Physical Chemistry. Its annual funding is 50,000 yuan, all subsidized by various parties, such as the Sichuan Provincial Bank, Minsheng Company, China Cultural Foundation, Beiping Geological Survey Institute, Academia Sinica, and Chief Supervisor Liu, etc.; (2) The Gorges Defense Regiment Affairs Bureau trains 500 members of the local militia for the purpose of preventing threats to mines and rural areas. The bureau also established a local hospital and a public education center, including a public night school, a boatmen's school, and a career placement center, etc.; (3) Within the public sports field, there are parks, libraries, zoos, museums, etc.

This Mission Here

Finally, Mr. Lu added that his most important mission in coming to Shanghai from Chongqing this time is to inspect the Shanghai branch of Minsheng Industrial Company. He will stay in Shanghai for about a month before returning to Sichuan. It is said that in addition to inspecting the Shanghai branch, Mr. Lu will also take the opportunity to investigate Shanghai's industries. General Manager Gongquan of the Bank of China, etc., will schedule a meeting.

Important Figures Travelled to the Capital Last Night to Meet Chairman Chiang Kai-shek, Who Will Come to Shanghai for a Short Rest

Chairman Chiang Kai-shek of the Military Affairs Commission returned to the capital yesterday morning to participate in the 10th-anniversary celebration of the military academy. Various important figures also went to the capital to gather. Elders Li Shih-tseng and Zhang Jingjiang, former Foreign Minister Wang Zhengting, Vice Foreign Minister Tang Youren, Secretary-General of the Executive Yuan Chu Minyi, Song Zi-liang, etc., took the 11 o'clock night train to Nanjing last night to meet Chairman Chiang Kai-shek. It is reported that Mr. Chiang plans to stay in the capital for a few days and then come to Shanghai before returning to his ancestral home in Fenghua or going to Hangzhou for a short rest. Huang Fu, chairman of the North China Reorganization Committee, has no plans to leave Shanghai recently and may wait until he has met with Mr. Chiang in Shanghai before returning north.

Tang Youren Arrived in Shanghai Yesterday, Saying the Kagemoto Incident is a Thing of the Past

The China Eastern News Agency reports that Vice Foreign Minister Tang Youren returned to Nanjing in a hurry from Jiangxi on the 13th. When Vice Consul Kagemoto was found, and after Consul General Suma paid his respects and apologies to Wang [Jingwei], the matter was superficially concluded on the 14th. Mr. Tang came to Shanghai by night train the day before yesterday to change his medicine. A reporter from the China Eastern News Agency paid a special visit to Mr. Tang at his residence yesterday, inquiring about the ins and outs of the Kagemoto incident. According to Mr. Tang, the matter is a thing of the past and he hopes that the people of the country will regard it as a fleeting cloud and not be concerned about it, forgetting it completely. Mr. Tang returned to Nanjing by night train on the same day due to being busy.

Kagemoto Incident, Huang Fu Expresses His Thoughts: Sharp Nerves Often Lead to Mistakes; Remaining Calm Often Leads to More Satisfactory Results

The New News Agency reports that after Kagemoto was found, a reporter from the New News Agency wanted to know the details of the incident and drove to visit Huang Fu, chairman of the Beiping Political Reorganization Committee, who was staying in Shanghai, to ask for his thoughts. He stated his thoughts as follows: After Vice Consul Kagemoto disappeared, both the Chinese and Japanese governments attached great importance to it. Fortunately, he was found by the military police in the capital, and Mr. Kagemoto is safe and sound. This is indeed a cause for celebration for both China and Japan. Before he was found, both Chinese and Japanese people inevitably made alarming speculations. Now that the doubts have been dispelled, we know that the previous speculations were excessive. Things in the world are often misled by sharp nerves. Who knows, under calm and composed circumstances, the result may be more satisfactory. What is particularly interesting to me is that Mr. Kagemoto, unable to endure hunger, went down the mountain to seek food. In his extreme distress, he sought comfort in resigning himself to his fate, yet he still adhered to his moral principles and was not opportunistic. He paid for his meal with a gold button. The owner of the small restaurant, who runs a small business, surprisingly did not accept the gold from the strange foreign guest whose language and appearance he did not recognize. The giving and receiving were conducted with courtesy and respect, which shows the nobility of Eastern morality and the depth of cultivation. If this kind of method and this kind of spirit are promoted in general international relations, and if both sides hold the highest standards of humanity, examine themselves, and adhere to rational principles, there will be no problems that cannot be resolved peacefully.

Kagemoto Left Beijing Yesterday Afternoon, Arriving in Shanghai This Afternoon to Enter Hospital for Treatment; Whether to Return to His Country Will Be Determined Based on His Condition

The New News Agency reports that, according to sources at the Japanese Embassy, Japanese Vice Consul Kagemoto Hideaki, who was stationed in Beijing, rested briefly in Beijing after being found after his disappearance, and then, following the instructions of Dr. Matsui, took the Japanese ship Nanyo Maru from Beijing to Shanghai at noon yesterday. He is expected to arrive in Shanghai this afternoon and will first enter the Fumin Hospital on North Sichuan Road to treat his neurasthenia. Whether he will return to his country will be determined after examining his condition. However, the Ministry of Foreign Affairs has not yet changed his position as vice consul, nor has it sent any telegrams to Beijing or Shanghai recalling him to his country. Eurasia Company Opens New Lanzhou-Ningxia Route, Scheduled to Officially Open on the 19th; Li Jingzong Returned to Shanghai from Jiangxi Yesterday

The Central News Agency reports that Mr. Li Jingzong, the general manager of the Eurasia Aviation Company, was summoned to Jiangxi by Chairman Chiang Kai-shek at the beginning of this month to inquire about aviation matters. He has now completed his mission and returned to Shanghai yesterday morning. A reporter from the Central News Agency visited Mr. Li at the company yesterday and inquired about his visit to Chiang in Jiangxi and the company's plan to open a new Lanzhou-Ningxia route. He spoke as follows:

Visit to Chiang in Jiangxi

According to Mr. Li, reports stating that his visit to Chiang Kai-shek in Jiangxi this time was to ask for instructions on the opening of the Eurasia route are not factual. His trip was purely at the invitation of Chiang Kai-shek. After arriving in Jiangxi and meeting with Chiang, he was asked in great detail about aviation matters. These aviation matters do not refer specifically to the Eurasia route, but the details are not yet ready to be announced.

Opening of the New Lanzhou-Ningxia Route

In order to develop transportation in the northwest, the company decided to open a new Lanzhou-Ningxia route. The route is 400 kilometers long, from Lanzhou to Ningxia, and can be reached in two hours. It is scheduled to officially open on the 19th of this month. The opening of this route was not planned in advance. During his last inspection of the Northwest, Song Ziwen, a standing member of the National Economic Commission, flew over the route on a Eurasia plane and believed that the route was very short, had a large population, and definitely needed to be added. Therefore, there will be no more test flights before the official opening. As for the schedule, flights will depart from Shanghai to Lanzhou every Tuesday, and then from Lanzhou to Ningxia. Every Friday, flights will depart from Ningxia to Lanzhou and then to Shanghai. The fare is set at over 200 yuan.

Trip to Xinjiang to Meet Sheng is Undecided

As for the completion of the Eurasia route, the situation in Xinjiang is not yet very clear. To this day, planes can only reach Lanzhou. Although the company has repeatedly sent telegrams to negotiate, it has not been effective. Recent news has it that Sheng Shicai, the governor of the province, is now running his own private airline within the province. According to a telegram from Sheng, the airline has been established and flies to the Hami-Tacheng route, and he has requested that Eurasia planes fly to Hami to facilitate connections. After receiving the telegram, Mr. Li believed that Sheng's move was related to the contract signed by the Ministry of Transportation and the German company for the Eurasia route. Therefore, he immediately sent a telegram stating his views and requesting to go to Dihua to meet with Sheng to discuss the matter in person. A month has passed since the telegram was sent, and no reply has been received. Therefore, he will send another telegram to request it so that the Eurasia route can be completed as soon as possible. As for the date of going to Xinjiang to meet with Sheng, it will be determined after the reply telegram arrives.

Commentary by the Central Bank Corporation on the Current State of China's Railways: Progress is Being Made and the Future is Optimistic

The New News Agency reports that the Sino-British Bank Corporation, a financial institution that invests in China's railways, is very familiar with the situation of China's railway administration. The company recently held its annual meeting, and Chairman Bernard reported that: (1) The Beining Railway was affected by the situation last year, and the Tianjin-Yushu section was not opened to traffic until August last year. The Shenyang-Yushu section of the railway was also occupied by the Japanese. However, the monthly income of the section within the customs area is still 800,000 yuan; (2) The income of the Shanghai-Nanjing Railway last year was about 13.5 million yuan, an increase of more than 4 million yuan compared with the previous year. The total surplus for the year was about 6 million yuan. The construction of the Shanghai Railway Station and the Nanjing Ferry cost a lot. The compensation and interest are paid monthly as scheduled; (3) The income of the Jinpu Railway last year was about 21 million yuan, an increase of 1 million yuan compared with the previous year. The total net surplus was 6 million yuan. The chairman concluded that although China's railway administration is in a very difficult environment, there are signs of progress and the future is optimistic.

Government Consults with China Travel Service to Undertake Through Train Service; The Company is Still Considering Carefully

The China Eastern News Agency reports that, according to reliable sources, there is no problem in principle with the through train service, but in terms of technical aspects, the organization of the commercial agency undertaking this matter has a major relationship with the principles. If this kind of agency is well organized, it can completely avoid the suspicion of contacting pseudo-agencies and can safeguard national sovereignty. It is said that although the agency is jointly organized by China and Japan, it must be in accordance with Chinese law. In the government's opinion, China favors China Travel Service. China Travel Service has a long history in society and is trusted by both China and foreign countries. If it is appointed to this matter, it will greatly benefit national sovereignty and status. The authorities have repeatedly consulted with the travel agency, hoping that the travel agency will prioritize the country and resolutely undertake the task. However, the company is still considering it carefully. Once it is resolved, it can be implemented.

The General Situation of China's Trade with Southeast Asia in the First Four Months of This Year: Trade Surplus with Singapore and the Philippines, But the Total Still Shows a Deficit of Over 50 Million

The Central News Agency reports that although China's trade with Southeast Asia is far less important than that with the United States, Britain, and Japan, the close economic relationship between Southeast Asia and China has attracted considerable attention from the Chinese people. The Bureau of International Trade has released the general situation of China's trade with Southeast Asia in the first, second, third, and fourth months of this year, which is recorded as follows:

Total Imports

In terms of total imports, the total imports from various places in Southeast Asia in the first four months of this year reached more than 62.3 million yuan, of which the most were from the Dutch East Indies, reaching more than 28.014 million yuan. Annam ranked second, reaching more than 15.665 million yuan. Siam ranked third, reaching more than 12.249 million yuan. Singapore and other places ranked fourth, with more than 4.379 million yuan. The Philippines ranked fifth, with more than 1.517 million yuan. British North Borneo had the least, with only more than 186,000 yuan.

Commodities

In terms of major imported commodities, the most imported commodity from the Dutch East Indies was kerosene, totaling 3,428,246 gold units. Sugar was second, totaling 2,981,239 gold units. Diesel oil was third, totaling 2,301,327 gold units. The main import from Annam was rice, totaling 5,904,309 gold units in the first four months. Coal was second, valued at 727,249 gold units. Rice accounted for 80-90% of the imports from Siam, totaling 5,346,507 gold units in the first four months. The main imports from Singapore and other places were rubber products, totaling 565,077 gold units. Timber was second, totaling 356,314 gold units. In addition, rattan products and seafood were also major imports from Singapore and other places. The imports from the Philippines were medicines and spices, totaling 202,389 gold units, and wood, bamboo, and rattan products, totaling 191,422 gold units. As for the imports from North Borneo, they were only a small amount of wood and rattan products. Overall, the largest imported commodity from Southeast Asia was rice, totaling 11.26 million gold units in four months, accounting for 94% of China's total rice imports, which shows the importance of Southeast Asian rice in China's grain market.

Total Exports

In terms of total exports, the total exports to major regions in Southeast Asia reached more than 11.251 million yuan, of which the most were to Singapore and other places, totaling more than 4.766 million yuan. The Dutch East Indies were second, totaling 1.275 million yuan. The Philippines were third, totaling 1.561 million yuan. Siam was next, totaling more than 1.44 million yuan. In addition, exports to Annam totaled more than 1.206 million yuan. As for British North Borneo, it was only more than 2,000 yuan.

Commodities

In terms of major exported commodities, the main exports to Singapore and other places were agricultural products and vegetables, totaling 55,381 yuan in the first four months. Paper, fruits, textiles, and clothing parts each reached more than 400,000 yuan. Cotton cloth, beans, tea, medicines, spices, and raw oil were also significant. The main export to the Dutch East Indies was cotton yarn, reaching 895,997 yuan in four months. Clothing parts were second, reaching 83,034 yuan. Silk and paper were also significant. The main export to the Philippines was also cotton yarn, totaling 349,003 yuan. Clothing parts were second, totaling 223,681 yuan. Cotton yarn accounted for the majority of exports to Siam, totaling 317,190 yuan. The main export to Annam was silk, totaling 280,946 yuan. Paper and silk fabrics also reached more than 100,000 yuan. Overall, the most exported commodity from China to various places in Southeast Asia was textiles, with a total export value of more than 5.41 million yuan in four months, accounting for about 30% of China's total textile exports, which shows that Southeast Asia is a major market for China's textiles.

Two Places with Trade Surplus

In terms of trade balance, China only had a trade surplus with Singapore and other places and the Philippines. In the first four months, the trade surplus with Singapore and other places was more than 387,000 yuan, and the trade surplus with the Philippines was more than 45,000 yuan. All other places had a trade deficit, especially the Dutch East Indies, which had the largest trade deficit, totaling more than 15.739 million yuan. Annam was second, totaling more than 14.459 million yuan. Siam was third, totaling more than 10.809 million yuan. In addition, British North Borneo also had a trade deficit with China, reaching more than 485,000 yuan. In the comparison of imports and exports in the first, second, third, and fourth months of this year, China's trade with Southeast Asia had a net trade deficit of more than 51.06 million yuan.

All North China Merchant Ships Will Implement Alliance Cooperation Tomorrow; Freight Rates and Commissions Are Still Being Negotiated; Implementation Methods Have Already Been Agreed Upon

Sixteen Chinese shipping companies, in order to save North China's shipping industry, have formed a cooperative alliance to increase freight rates and unify shipping fees. This matter was reported in yesterday's newspaper. Now, the joint unity of the companies and the request for foreign shipping companies to join have been actively carried out. The news that this newspaper reporter continued to obtain is described in detail below.

Cooperation Methods

The cooperation methods of the 18 Chinese and foreign shipping companies have been agreed upon by the representatives of the various shipping companies. After being unanimously approved, each shipping company will send one responsible representative to form a joint office. Five representatives will be selected from the representatives to serve as executive members of the joint office, and the remaining representatives will serve as supervisory members. It is stipulated that each company must first pay a deposit of 2,000 yuan to the office, which will be deposited in the bank in the name of the executive members. If it is to be withdrawn, it must be signed by all the executive members before it can be withdrawn.

Increase Freight Rates

The allied companies decided to increase shipping fees, starting with rice and flour, appropriately increasing freight rates, and then continuing to discuss the increase in freight rates for groceries. The allied companies will set uniform commissions and must abide by the shipping rates set by the joint office. After that, there must be no more temporary declines in prices in secret. The joint office may send supervisory members to the various shipping companies to inspect books and accounts. If they object to the inspection or violate the agreed-upon shipping rates, the office may confiscate their 2,000 yuan deposit.

Exchange Bills of Lading

If the allied shipping companies load rice, grain, and wheat flour, they must send a report to the association and notify the various companies after three days to facilitate exchange. For the convening of the general meeting, two-thirds of the executive members must be present, and the proposal can be passed with the consent of more than half of them. In the event of a dispute, it shall be resolved by the association hiring an impartial person to mediate. Representatives of companies involved in disputes have no right to speak.

Implementation Period

The implementation period for the alliance cooperation of the 18 companies is tentatively set for one year. When the period expires, it will be submitted to the meeting for discussion. If two-thirds of them pass, it can be decided to continue or dissolve it. As for the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company joining the alliance, it had previously stated that it must first conduct a trial for one month. If it is effective during the trial period, the contract will be supplemented and signed to continue the alliance. Jardine Matheson and Butterfield & Swire will first conduct a 14-day trial and then sign a contract to join.

Freight Rates and Commissions

Yesterday's newspaper recorded the new freight rates for rice and grain and wheat flour, as well as the method for giving commissions to customs brokers. This reporter has learned that the new freight rates are still being discussed, and the amount of commission has not yet been determined. The rates and commissions must be discussed with the customs brokerage industry. It cannot be decided unilaterally. After it is officially decided, a unified method will be announced.

This Municipal Public Bond

The Shenshi News Agency reports that the municipal government is issuing construction bonds worth 3.5 million yuan purely for the purpose of developing the city. The bonds were approved by the Zhongzheng Conference on the 12th. After the Legislative Yuan reviews and decides, they can be officially issued by September of this year at the latest. Once the issuance method of the bonds is passed by the Legislative Yuan and officially approved for issuance, a underwriting contract can be signed with the banking syndicate. At that time, the municipal government will submit it to the Executive Yuan for approval.

Delineation of Boundaries Between Shanghai, Songjiang, and Nanhui Counties is Underway; Shanghai County Mainly Delineates the Songjiang-Nanhui Border Area

Miao Qiping, commissioned by the Jiangsu Provincial Government, has come to investigate the issue of the boundary delineation between Shanghai, Songjiang, and Nanhui counties. It is learned that this case originated from the third administrative meeting held by Shanghai County last month. Members Huang Yunshun and Jiang Shijie proposed that the current area of the county is less than 500 square li and the population is less than 110,000. It is found that Zhuanqiao, Fengzhen, Zhujiaxiang, Changqiao, and other places belonging to Songjiang County are far away from Songjiang City. In order to facilitate administration, they should be劃歸 under the jurisdiction of Shanghai County. In addition, the nine townships, including Zhongxinhe, belonging to Nanhui County should also be劃歸 under the jurisdiction of Shanghai County. It was resolved to present the reasons in detail by the county and request the provincial government to re-劃歸. Now, Provincial Commissioner Miao has been accompanied by Pan Zhongjia, the county magistrate of Shanghai County, Jin Tigan, the county magistrate of Songjiang County, and Yuan Xiluo, the county magistrate of Nanhui County, as well as the district chiefs of the disputed areas, to conduct investigations separately. However, the people of Songjiang and Nanhui counties oppose the re-劃歸 and demand that the original state be maintained, and each submitted a petition. The people of Nanhui County, on the other hand, demanded that Sanlin, Chenhang, and other places belonging to Shanghai County be劃歸 under the jurisdiction of Nanhui County, on the grounds that although these two places are under the jurisdiction of Shanghai, they are separated by the Huangpu River and should be劃歸 under the jurisdiction of Nanhui County according to their natural form. Commissioner Miao recorded the investigation separately and drew a map of the terrain, which will be returned to the province for review. It is unknown how it will be resolved in the future.

Shanghai Chamber of Commerce Letter to Concession Authorities: Request to Postpone Pressing for Renovation of Street-Facing Buildings

The Shanghai General Chamber of Commerce yesterday sent a letter to the Municipal Bureau of Public Works, the British Concession's Public Works Department, and the French Concession's Municipal Council, stating: "To Whom It May Concern: On the 14th of this month, we received a letter from the Shanghai Pawnshop Association stating that rents in Shanghai are already high, and miscellaneous expenses are also substantial. Since the January 28th Incident, the market has declined daily, and prices have plummeted. In addition, the dumping of foreign goods has led to the near bankruptcy of most industrial and commercial businesses, with many already feeling unable to maintain operations. They are doing their best to weather the storm by economizing, but housing costs are a major expenditure. Many businesses cannot afford rent, and their rent arrears are growing. Landlords are renovating city properties hoping to revive the market, but this only leads to higher rents, making it even harder for businesses to lease. City properties are closing, affecting the city's appearance. We only wish that when raising rents, they would consider the difficulties businesses face in operating. We would like to request that you forward this letter to the Municipal Bureau of Public Works, the British Public Works Department, and the French Municipal Council, requesting that they temporarily postpone pressing for the renovation of street-facing buildings, so as to temporarily maintain the market and protect industrial and commercial businesses. We have observed that landlords, in order to increase rental income, are renovating buildings that are not yet particularly old and renting them out to new tenants. This self-serving behavior has become almost a common practice. While this may be related to revitalizing the market, in reality, rents are only getting higher, further exacerbating business difficulties. Based on the aforementioned circumstances, we respectfully request that your bureaus consider the current economic hardship and, in the future, when landlords apply for renovation permits, if their buildings have not reached the point where renovation is absolutely necessary, handle the matter strictly. Regarding the renovation of street-facing buildings, unless the construction poses a genuine safety hazard, we also request that you temporarily postpone urging landlords to renovate in order to alleviate business difficulties. We would be most grateful."

Women's National Products Year: Joint Meeting of Design and Economic Committees; Holding a National Products Exhibition at Various Girls' Schools; Requesting National Products Stores to Indicate Manufacturer's Trademark

Resolutions: (1) Proposal to amend the committee's work outline for the second half of the year: (Resolved) To be submitted to the Design Committee for design and voted on at the next meeting. (Resolved) To widely solicit paintings from artists for display, with the committee providing prizes to encourage participation. (3) How to encourage women and children to use national products? (4) Should national products companies be requested to indicate the manufacturer's trademark? (Resolved) The committee should send a letter to the Shanghai General Chamber of Commerce, forwarded to various national products companies and stores, requesting them to indicate the manufacturer's factory number and trademark on the goods they sell so that buyers can identify them. (5) How to hold a national products exhibition at various girls' schools? (Resolved) The committee will prepare to contact factories and schools, with Zhu Wang Wanqing, Huang Bingpei, Pan Tang Guanyu, Lin Kecong, Li Manyun, Fei Xia, Zhou Xixin and others representing the promotion efforts. (6) How to handle the surplus funds from the West Shanghai market? (Resolved) The committee will retain the funds for temporary national products promotion expenses. (7) Should the National Products Promotion Vehicle be actively promoted by the China and Shanghai National Products Companies and various national products factories? (Resolved) Approved. (8) The addition of Mrs. Cao Fengxiang, wife of Qian Xinzhi, as an economic committee member, and Ms. Zhou Xixin and Ms. Fei Xia as work committee members? (Resolved) Approved.

Ministry of Transportation Promulgates Rules for Motorized Rowboats

Yesterday, an order was issued to the Shanghai Navigation Administration Bureau to comply.

The Shanghai Navigation Administration Bureau yesterday received an order from the Ministry of Transportation promulgating thirteen articles of rules for the regulation of motorized rowboats. The original text is as follows: Article 1: All rowboats operated by mechanical power shall comply with these rules. Article 2: Motorized rowboats shall be limited to a total tonnage of 20 tons or less. Article 3: Motorized rowboats shall apply for measurement and inspection in accordance with the regulations for the measurement, inspection, registration, and licensing of small steamers. If they comply with these rules, the competent navigation administration bureau shall issue a certificate and apply for a license in accordance with the regulations. Article 4: Motorized rowboats shall have the following equipment: (1) Passenger cabin and engine room canopy; (2) Steering gear; (3) Red and green side lights; (4) Life-saving and fire-fighting equipment; (5) Steam whistle. Article 5: The canopy in item 1 of the previous article shall be made of materials that can block wind and rain and are not easily flammable. The life-saving and fire-fighting equipment in item 4 shall be marked with the name of the shipowner and the ship's name. Article 6: The hull of a motorized rowboat shall be sturdy and free from seepage or leakage. The arrangement of the machinery shall be suitable for the condition of the ship, so that there is no violent vibration during navigation and no excessive tilting during operation. Article 7: The engine room and passenger cabin of a motorized rowboat must be completely separated. Article 8: Motorized rowboats must have adequate ballast in the hold when necessary. Article 9: Cargo or luggage shall not be loaded on the canopy of a motorized rowboat. Article 10: After obtaining the measurement and inspection certificate, if a motorized rowboat is damaged due to a collision or disaster, or when the machinery is replaced, a temporary inspection shall be requested. Article 11: Applications for measurement, inspection, and licensing of motorized rowboats shall be subject to fees in accordance with the provisions of the attached schedule to the regulations for the measurement, inspection, registration, and licensing of small steamers. Article 12: If a motorized rowboat violates the provisions of Article 3 or Article 10, the competent navigation administration bureau may prohibit its navigation, and if it has a certificate or license, it may also detain the certificate. Article 13: These rules shall take effect from the date of promulgation.

China Merchants Steam Navigation Company's "Puan" Vessel: Dispute over Tips Resolved Yesterday

A dispute over tips between the workers in the third and fourth-class cabins of the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company's "Puan" vessel and the steward, Situ Langchuan, was formally resolved yesterday through mediation by the Seamen's Union with the signing of an agreement. The details are as follows:

Dispute over Distribution of Tips

The "Puan" vessel was leased by the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company from the Navy Department last year and began operating on the Shanghai-Qingdao and Shanghai-Putuo lines. The steward, Situ Langchuan, hired workers to serve passengers in the first, second, third, and fourth-class cabins. When the workers first started working on the vessel, the steward determined whether to allow workers to pay a deposit or not based on whether they had credit. Those who paid a deposit paid different amounts, such as thirty, fifty, or one hundred yuan. The workers also had to pay 80% of the tips they received from serving passengers to the steward. Later, the workers felt that they only received 20% of the tips each time, which was not enough to live on, so they had a dispute with the steward. The workers in the first and second-class cabins resolved the dispute themselves after both parties agreed a month ago. However, due to the steward dismissing Liu Awei and two others on trumped-up charges, the opinions of both sides became increasingly polarized. The China Merchants Steam Navigation Company and the General Seamen's Union mediated several times, but without results.

Signing of Resolution Method

Yesterday, the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company specially dispatched Section Chief Yao, together with Seamen's Union members Jiao Bolin, Shanghai Branch members Lu　Zhi, Lü Shuangxi, Secretary Si Shijian, and staff member Song Xiaoyun, to convene a mediation session and sign the following agreement: (1) The distribution of tips will temporarily follow the "five-five" and "four-five" distribution, i.e., 55% for the workers and 45% for the steward, Situ Yuchuan, and all miscellaneous expenses will not be borne by the workers (This section only applies to third and fourth-class cabins; the first and second-class cabins will continue to follow the "five-five" custom). (2) The deposits paid by the workers must be deposited with the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company, or the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company will be responsible for returning them. (3) Whether Liu Awei and the other two have committed any errors will be investigated and handled by the union within one voyage. During the investigation period, the three will leave the ship for one voyage. If it is found that they have not committed any errors that warrant dismissal, they will return to work on the ship after one voyage. (4) The steward, Situ Langchuan, shall not hire new workers, thereby reducing the livelihood of the original members. The current quota is twelve, and it shall not be changed easily. However, if it is necessary to hire new workers due to business reasons, the approval of the bureau must be obtained, and the union may introduce members to be selected by the steward.

[P>Manufacturers in Penglai Market Oppose Landlord Increasing Rent; Organize a Petition Delegation; Submit to the Municipal Government Requesting Prohibition

The Penglai Market in the South City was built with the sole investment of Kuang Zhongmou, who promoted it as a way to promote national products and prosper the market. He invited domestic manufacturers to rent shops and set up stores. Over the years, it has become the only national products market in the South District. The rent was initially ten yuan per room, then increased to fifteen yuan. After the January 28th Incident, it increased to twenty yuan. Recently, Kuang Zhongmou, the owner of the market, plans to continue to increase the rent. The manufacturers and stores believe that at a time when the market is sluggish, business is declining, and the entire city is carrying out rent reduction movements, the market is actually proposing a rent increase, which is an intentional attempt to destroy the national products business. They have expressed their opposition and organized a petition delegation, which yesterday jointly submitted a petition to the municipal government and the municipal party headquarters, and sent letters to the municipal chamber of commerce and other groups, requesting them to find ways to stop the rent increase and provide righteous assistance.

Lantern and Garden Party Held at Xu Garden for the Dragon Boat Festival

The Lantern and Garden Party held by the Xiehe Company at the Xu Garden on Kang Nao Tuo Road for the Dragon Boat Festival ended yesterday. It is reported that the ticket price was only thirty cents in order to be accessible to the public. Therefore, gentlemen and ladies from near and far flocked to visit. Yesterday was the first day of the opening. From morning to night, tourists flocked to the garden, with shoulders rubbing against each other and heels bumping into each other, creating a crowded scene. The deserted and desolate Kang Nao Tuo Road was transformed into a bustling and noisy city with heavy traffic. The garden was full of lanterns and streamers. At night, the lights were dazzling and eye-catching. The most eye-catching things in the garden were the two green and white divine snakes, which were said to have been produced in the Five Sparrow Mountain in Quzhou, Zhejiang. They were purchased at a high price and transported to Shanghai for display. The white snake was pure white, like bright jade, while the green snake was emerald green, like green jade. They were truly rare objects in the world. According to legend, the ancient books said that the White Lady and Xiaoqing came down to earth. Although this is close to superstition, it is also a coincidence. In order to avoid congestion, the association has specially issued snake viewing tickets attached to the entrance tickets, allowing visitors to visit in order. However, people were still scrambling to get in, causing congestion. The dragon boat on land, which was said to have been made by Empress Dowager Cixi of the late Qing Dynasty, was exquisitely constructed, with interlocking corners and meticulous craftsmanship. It was truly a spectacle. There was also a rolling dragon boat, which was even more brilliant and superb, with lively eyebrows and dancing eyes, making people exclaim in admiration. Today is the Dragon Boat Festival according to the lunar calendar. It is expected that there will be even more tourists today than yesterday. However, the event will only last for two days, so the opportunity will not come again.

Pan Xulun Talks About Xinhua Village

Since the news of the construction of Xinhua Village was released, all sectors of society have paid close attention. According to accountant Pan Xulun, the village is located on the West Sports Association Road, which can be said to be the Yuyuan Road of Shanghai's eastern district. The air is clean, the scenery is beautiful, the transportation is convenient, and the equipment is complete. It has the convenience of a city and the pleasure of a countryside. The new village has a small vegetable market and a small school, which can save residents the trouble of traveling and provide children with a good education. I (Pan Xiansheng calls himself) have always paid close attention to living conditions. Because our mental fullness, mental flexibility, and work efficiency are all closely related to where we live. The British and American people regard housing as one of the most important things in life. Therefore, when building houses, they must choose excellent environments, which is why they are physically strong and mentally energetic. We Chinese are the sick men of East Asia. Now, Xinhua Village is truly an ideal place to live. Living there will definitely benefit the body and mind. Another thing is that the purchase of land and houses in Xinhua Village is done through installment payments, which are paid back monthly, making it easy to pay off the house money. After a few years, the houses and land will all be self-produced, and the housing problem will be solved forever, which is very good. Therefore, I have already ordered two lots of land in the village and decided to build a house to solve my own housing problem.

Hongqiao Sanatorium, to be Completed Tomorrow, Founded by Ding Fubao Personally; Mayor Wu to Perform Opening Ceremony

The Hongqiao Sanatorium was founded by Mr. Ding Fubao of Wuxi to meet the needs of the medical community. It is located on Hongqiao Road in the quietest part of western Shanghai. The site has ample sunlight, fresh air, beautiful flowers and trees, and is free from dust and noise. It faces southeast, has pleasant scenery, and convenient transportation. It is indeed an ideal sanatorium. It is heard that the sanatorium will be completed tomorrow at 3 p.m., and Mayor Wu will hold the opening ceremony, inviting Chinese and foreign doctors and guests. At that time, Hongqiao Road will be bustling with traffic and will surely be a grand occasion.

Grand Architecture

The sanatorium is a cuboid building with stepped rooms. The entire structure is built with reinforced concrete, and the construction is solid, fireproof, and soundproof. The sanatorium bedrooms face completely south, providing ample sunlight and air. Each room has a separate balcony and hot and cold water pipes. In addition to various medical rooms, the sanatorium also has a sunbathing terrace, a lounge, a dining room, a music room, a library, etc. The interior and exterior facilities are simple and beautiful, and its location in the suburbs makes it even more majestic.

Latest Equipment

The sanatorium's sun lamp room was custom-made in Germany and can accommodate sixteen people for irradiation at the same time. The special wards are equipped with ultraviolet glass windows, so even in bad weather, the collected light will still be effective. The X-ray machine is the world's latest invention with shock-absorbing equipment. The short-wave electrotherapy machine is also the latest invention in medicine and has a huge therapeutic effect. The operating room adopts shadowless lighting equipment. All bedroom furniture is made of stainless steel for easy disinfection. The operating room and special wards are also equipped with cold air conditioning. All kinds of equipment can be said to be the most modern in sanatoriums in East Asia.

Doctor Luo Pin

The sanatorium adopts the latest methods in terms of treatment and equipment. Whether chemical, physical, stimulating, or other new therapies, all can be implemented. In addition to hiring chemical examination, X-ray specialists, and experienced Chinese and Western nurses, the sanatorium also employs famous doctors from Shanghai to preside over medical affairs and organizes a board of directors to manage the sanatorium professionally.

After Divorcing His Wife, Ye Xunruo Sues to Affirm Invalidity; Loses First Trial and Now Appeals; Opposing Party Unwilling to Reconcile

Ye Xunruo from Ningbo is a member of the same clan as the late Ye Chengzhong, who donated his wealth to promote education, and is from a wealthy family. However, he is inherently addicted to gambling and prostitution. After marrying Zhu Wenjuan, he continued his ways, indulging in drinking and gambling, and seeking pleasure with prostitutes, and the family's fortunes gradually declined. Although his wife repeatedly advised him, he rarely repented. Therefore, Zhu felt unwilling to live with him until old age, as he was immersed in pleasure. She hired a lawyer years ago to negotiate a divorce. After discussion, a divorce agreement was signed, and their relationship was terminated. The children born were to be raised by Ye, and Zhu would not interfere. Ye promised to repay 10,000 yuan of Zhu's private savings that he had used. Later, because Ye failed to repay the debt as scheduled, Zhu filed a lawsuit against Ye, requesting a judgment ordering the defendant to pay the 10,000 yuan debt. Initially, it did not involve the marriage issue. Unexpectedly, Ye, when sued, suddenly filed a lawsuit against Zhu Wenjuan, demanding confirmation that the previously signed divorce agreement was invalid. From then on, the debt dispute turned into a divorce case. After the first instance trial by the First Special District Court concluded, it was ruled that the divorce agreement had the signatures of both parties and was certified by the lawyers hired by both parties, and the procedures were not inconsistent. How could it be overturned afterward? The plaintiff was ruled to have lost. However, Ye was very dissatisfied and appealed to the Second Branch of the Jiangsu High Court. Yesterday afternoon, three judges, Han, Jiang, and Cai, specially convened a collegiate panel to hear the case. The appellee, Zhu Wenjuan, was absent. The lawyer representing the appellant, Ye Xunruo, stated the grounds for the appeal, saying that Ye really did not want to divorce his wife and requested that Zhu be summoned to court so that Ye could meet with her and attempt a reconciliation. The lawyer representing Zhu Wenjuan replied that Zhu was absolutely unwilling to meet with Ye again. The divorce agreement was signed with the full consent of both parties at the time, and the procedures were handled very carefully. If Ye hoped to reunite, he would have to hire a matchmaker again and remarry. However, this was not something that the law could remedy, nor could the lawyer or the presiding judge advise. He requested that the appeal be rejected. The court then questioned Ye about the circumstances of signing the agreement. According to Ye, he signed it at Cai's law firm. He had no lawyer at first, and although he was not forced to sign, Cai's words were very serious at the time, and he had to sign. After the contract was handed over to his three lawyers for review, they said that he had been fooled, but there was no way to remedy it. After the court finished questioning, it ordered that the date of the judgment be announced later.

Young Woman Assassinated in Inn on Balijiao Street; Man Seizes Opportunity to Flee; Young Woman Already Stabbed to Death

Last night, a young woman was murdered in an inn on Balijiao Street (i.e., West Xinjiao Street) in the French Concession. Details are recorded below:

Place of Secret Rendezvous

The Rongxing Inn at 335 Balijiao Street, outside Xiaobeimen in the French Concession, is owned by Yang Xie, a woman from Ningbo (41 years old). It has been open for many years. Although small in scale, the business is doing quite well. In reality, it is a place for temporary secret rendezvous for lower-class men and women.

Man and Woman Arrive Together

Yesterday at around 4 p.m., two young customers, a man and a woman, suddenly arrived at the inn. The man looked like a worker, and the woman looked like a maid. The man signed his name as Zhu Axing, 26 years old, and the woman's name was Zhu Lu, 24 years old. Both were from Anhui and made a living by rowing boats. After entering the inn, the waiter Wang Afu led them to room number 4 upstairs. They paid a room fee of 40 cents.

Man Leaves First

After the room fee was paid, the waiter Wang Afu, as usual, brewed tea and brought it along with the washing water, and then left. There was nothing unusual at the time. After a while, the sound of laughter was heard from the two. Two hours later, at about 6:15 p.m., the man called the waiter Afu to buy two bowls of salty rice porridge. About ten minutes after the waiter left, one of the men and women suddenly stepped out of the room, talking to himself, and left.

Tragic Scene on the Bed

Before long, the waiter Wang Afu had bought the salty rice porridge. When he entered the room and looked around, the man was gone. At first, he suspected that he had gone out for something and would return soon. After waiting for about ten minutes and still not seeing him return, Afu entered the room to wake up the woman. Unexpectedly, she did not respond no matter how often he called. Knowing that something was wrong, he quickly opened the curtains. He saw that the woman was naked, with only one sock on her foot, and blood was flowing from her neck.

Stabbed Ten Times in Total

Seeing this, Afu was extremely frightened and shouted loudly. The innkeeper and other staff members entered the room together to check. She was already dead. They quickly reported to the constable, who immediately dispatched Chinese and Western detectives to investigate. It was estimated that there were ten stab wounds on the head and neck, and two stab wounds on the wrist. He immediately notified the Tongren Fuyuan Branch Examination Office and ordered the mortician to carry the body to the examination office to await a report to the Second Special Court for examination.

Huo Brothers Axe Dong Couple; Reason is Huo Ruiting's Lost Wife; Result is Dong Daofang Couple Injured

Yesterday (the 15th) at 5:10 a.m., near Jisifeier Road and Kaina Road in western Shanghai, inside Rongqing Lane 56, next to the Chinese Bank dormitory, a case of brothers wielding axes to kill a couple occurred. The two victims suffered a total of 23 stab wounds. The man was already dead, and the woman was also in critical condition. Blood was flowing everywhere, and the scene was too horrible to look at. The details obtained are recorded below:

Thugs Arrive Suddenly in Sweet Dreams

Dong Daofang from Xuzhou, 40 years old, worked in a yarn factory. His wife, Wang, 34 years old, also worked in the yarn factory's weaving room. The couple lived together in the front building of Rongqing Lane 56. Yesterday at 5:10 a.m., as the couple was sleeping soundly in bed, the landlord downstairs happened to open the door to empty the chamber pot. Two thugs suddenly rushed in and went straight upstairs, breaking down the door. The couple was awakened from their dreams.

Strength No Match for Double Axes

When the Dong couple saw two people each holding a sharp axe, they knew they had come to cause trouble. They jumped up and were about to question them, but the axes were already coming down, hacking fiercely. Although Dong tried his best to resist, because he was one against two, Wang was injured and fell to the ground first. Seeing that Wang had fallen, Dong, still injured, grappled with the two thugs to the hall downstairs. Due to exhaustion, his neck was cut off and he fainted. Seeing that their goal had been achieved, the two murderers fled quickly. The neighbors immediately telephoned the Haige Road Red Cross Hospital to send an ambulance to take Dong and Wang back to the hospital.

Blood Stains Everywhere Upstairs and Downstairs

Tan, the district chief of the sixth district, received the report and immediately dispatched Inspector Cheng and the detective team leader Wu Kezhong, deputy team leader Dong Wenrui, and detectives Yang Qing and Wu Yihe to rush to the scene. They found bloodstains everywhere upstairs and downstairs in the front building, and questioned the landlord. They also went to the hospital and saw that Dong had five or six stab wounds on his face and head, his neck bone had been cut off, and his arms, shoulders, and back were also injured in five or six places. He had already died. Wang's cheek was cut off, and there were about seven or eight wounds on her head, neck, hands, and chest. She was unconscious and on the verge of death. The two victims suffered a total of twenty-three wounds.

Murderers are Two Brothers

After detectives Wu and Dong conducted an investigation, they learned that the murderers were Huo Ruiting and Huo Ruilan, two brothers from Shandong who lived in the pavilion room at 131 in the same lane. The reason was that Huo Ruiting's wife, Chen, worked in the same factory as Dong's wife, Wang, and they knew each other. On the 5th of this month, they went to see the temple fair in Caojiadu together. After that, Chen suddenly disappeared. Huo searched everywhere, but there was no trace of her. He repeatedly negotiated with Dong and Wang, accusing Dong of plotting against her. Therefore, he resorted to this cruel act to seek revenge. District Chief Tan ordered all detectives and police officers to tighten their grip on the two murderers and arrest them for punishment.

Reading Q&A

The Interest in Reading Literary Books 丨丨Answer to Gu Nianchun and Li Xingyu丨丨

Before talking about the main text, I would like to talk to readers about something else. A year ago, I went to a middle school in a certain inland area to teach Chinese. When I first arrived, the friend who introduced me (also a Chinese teacher) specifically said to me, "The students here have very old-fashioned minds. Most of them still want to read classical Chinese, so the textbooks used are also classical Chinese selections published by a certain bookstore." I asked him what was the reason, and he replied, "They can understand vernacular Chinese at a glance and don't feel any interest, but classical Chinese is not..." I didn't express my opinion at the time, but I always felt that his words were not entirely true. The so-called interest is definitely not something that is born and cannot be transferred, and the teacher should not cater to the students' interest and lead them into the quagmire. So, on the one hand, I negotiated with the school authorities that the Chinese classes I taught would not use textbooks, and I would compile lecture notes; on the other hand, I devised a plan myself, first selecting some articles from the May Fourth era "and classical Chinese, and then selecting a few literary essays, with a few pure literary works attached. The intention was to first break their prejudice against classical Chinese, and then make them understand the true meaning of literature. Sure enough, my plan worked. In the first few weeks, some people did object and asked to read classical Chinese, but later this situation gradually decreased; in less than half a year, even the old teacher who taught classical Chinese was driven away by the students, creating a new literary atmosphere in the school.

It is very easy to get the answer by using this fact to explain the question of Gu and Li's interest in reading.

Mr. Gu said that 丨丨After reading a few literary books, I found them boring and tasteless, and interrupted my interest in reading.

Mr. Li said that 丨丨I love to read Gong Yuzhi's novels, but I don't love to read Lu Xun and Mao Dun's novels.

Obviously, the crux of the two gentlemen lies in the fact that they do not know how to receive interest from literary books, or because of the weakness of their perception. The deciding point lies in their lives and their literacy in literature.

Villagers think that it is the most boring thing to see students in the city playing football. Even if they occasionally kick one or two feet out of curiosity, they may even end up with leg pain and back pain. However, in the eyes of general sports-loving students, playing ball is more interesting than anything else. What is the reason for this? This is not about the characteristics of a certain person, it is because of their different daily lives that they have developed different interests. Of course, there are also people who are interested in events that are contrary to their special lives. For example, the children of scholarly families often do not want to study but like to fool around, and people who live in tall buildings prefer to swim in the water. This is a common phenomenon. However, it can still only be explained by their lives. The occurrence of these interests is a reflection of their lives. They are dissatisfied or tired of their own lives, and they are interested in the "Lord" interest.

Secondly, in the situation of "life", the interest of each person is still different in doing something, which is entirely because of the difference in the degree of understanding of something. A child who is just starting school often wants to rely on learning, but there are many scholars who can't even eat and can't stop him from reading. Regarding this, some people may wonder, "Why do people 'like the new and dislike the old'?" I can answer that this is human curiosity. Curiosity can lead to interest, but curiosity has nothing to do with interest. An old gentleman goes to a dance floor to watch dancing entirely out of curiosity. If he says that he is interested in dancing because of this, then it is a wrong. Talking about the true meaning of his article to a person who has just recognized "zhiwu" will naturally give rise to the feeling of playing the piano to a cow; if he only has the strength to bear a weight of fifty catties, and he wants to make him carry a burden of one hundred catties, then he can only force people to walk on the road to death.

Based on the above explanation, it can be seen that it is not worth being surprised that Gu and Li cannot arouse interest in reading literary books, but there are actually their own reasons; due to the author's experience (such as the facts mentioned above), to solve this problem 丨Improve your interest in reading literary books, on the one hand, you need to make your life closer to literature, on the other hand, you must not think of "reaching the sky in one step" but learn that "step by step" step by step, of course, this is not an easy thing. (To be continued)

Education News

Two Departments Stipulate Military Training Scoring Method

Failure to Pass Prohibits Promotion or Graduation

(Nanjing, 15th) The Training Supervision Department and the Education Department will jointly stipulate the key points of the scoring method for military training results above the high school level within days: (1) Military training is divided into technical and academic subjects; (2) The total score of technical studies is 60 points to pass, and those who fail to pass shall not be promoted or graduated; (3) The total score of military training is calculated by combining the three items of daily points, summer training and collective training.

Jiangxi High School Graduates Implement Summer Military Training

Gather in the Province to Form a Team on the 29th

Training Begins on July 1

This year's graduates from high schools and above in Jiangxi Province have decided to first inspect the physical condition of each student on June 29 and 30, and start military training on July 1. Students from other counties are allowed to purchase train and ship tickets for free or at half price. The procedures for entering the camp are as follows: (1) Registration Date: The schools will create a list of students undergoing training by the principals and send it to the meeting before June 18. The students will report to the meeting on June 29 by the leading personnel. (2) Date of Entering the Camp: June 29, wait for inspection and formation (3) Training Period: From July 1 to 31, i.e., an enlistment ceremony will be held on the day the training begins. (4) Items to Carry: Only daily necessities, diary, pencil, and two sets of simple summer clothes will be issued by the meeting for each person, and the military uniform will be returned after the expiration. Compensation will be paid for loss.

Focus on Diseases and Insect Pests

(Jinan, 14th) Zeng Shengzhi, Dean of the Agricultural College of Shandong University, talked about the fact that the college decided to open in Jinan in July, setting up agronomy, horticulture, and diseases and insect pests. Because Shandong is a cotton-producing area, it is decided to jointly form a cotton insect research institute with the Central Cotton Improvement Institute in Jinan.

Jinhua Primary School Principals Resign Collectively

Due to Meager Salaries and Huge Arrears

The principals of all county-run primary schools in Jinhua County, due to meager salaries and huge arrears, have no solution so far. At 1:00 pm on the 13th, the principals held a meeting at Zhengyi Primary School and decided on four measures: (1) The teachers of each school said that their salaries were meager and there was no guarantee. They asked for the arrears to be paid so that they could resign and seek another life. There was no solution so far, and they should resign unanimously. (2) Please ask the bureau to send someone to take over within three days, and will not be responsible if the deadline is exceeded (3) The arrears of salary before June 15 will be required to be paid in full by June 15, and if they are not paid by the deadline, they will sit and demand payment together with the teachers (4) All teachers and teachers will organize a salary-demanding group, and the principals will petition the county government, and the secretary will meet with them. The result was satisfactory, and the final decision will be made after County Mayor Li returns to Jinhua.

Also, within 24 hours before 3:00 pm yesterday, the highest temperature in this port was 78.6, and the lowest was 68.0. On the same day last year, the highest was 79.3 and the lowest was 70.7.

Reading Q&A

The Interest in Reading Literary Books 丨丨Answer to Gu Nianchun and Li Xingyu丨丨

Before talking about the main text, I would like to talk to readers about something else. A year ago, I went to a middle school in a certain inland area to teach Chinese. When I first arrived, the friend who introduced me (also a Chinese teacher) specifically said to me, "The students here have very old-fashioned minds. Most of them still want to read classical Chinese, so the textbooks used are also classical Chinese selections published by a certain bookstore." I asked him what was the reason, and he replied, "They can understand vernacular Chinese at a glance and don't feel any interest, but classical Chinese is not..." I didn't express my opinion at the time, but I always felt that his words were not entirely true. The so-called interest is definitely not something that is born and cannot be transferred, and the teacher should not cater to the students' interest and lead them into the quagmire. So, on the one hand, I negotiated with the school authorities that the Chinese classes I taught would not use textbooks, and I would compile lecture notes; on the other hand, I devised a plan myself, first selecting some articles from the May Fourth era "and classical Chinese, and then selecting a few literary essays, with a few pure literary works attached. The intention was to first break their prejudice against classical Chinese, and then make them understand the true meaning of literature. Sure enough, my plan worked. In the first few weeks, some people did object and asked to read classical Chinese, but later this situation gradually decreased; in less than half a year, even the old teacher who taught classical Chinese was driven away by the students, creating a new literary atmosphere in the school.

It is very easy to get the answer by using this fact to explain the question of Gu and Li's interest in reading.

Mr. Gu said that 丨丨After reading a few literary books, I found them boring and tasteless, and interrupted my interest in reading.

Mr. Li said that 丨丨I love to read Gong Yuzhi's novels, but I don't love to read Lu Xun and Mao Dun's novels.

Obviously, the crux of the two gentlemen lies in the fact that they do not know how to receive interest from literary books, or because of the weakness of their perception. The deciding point lies in their lives and their literacy in literature.

Villagers think that it is the most boring thing to see students in the city playing football. Even if they occasionally kick one or two feet out of curiosity, they may even end up with leg pain and back pain. However, in the eyes of general sports-loving students, playing ball is more interesting than anything else. What is the reason for this? This is not about the characteristics of a certain person, it is because of their different daily lives that they have developed different interests. Of course, there are also people who are interested in events that are contrary to their special lives. For example, the children of scholarly families often do not want to study but like to fool around, and people who live in tall buildings prefer to swim in the water. This is a common phenomenon. However, it can still only be explained by their lives. The occurrence of these interests is a reflection of their lives. They are dissatisfied or tired of their own lives, and they are interested in the "Lord" interest.

Secondly, in the situation of "life", the interest of each person is still different in doing something, which is entirely because of the difference in the degree of understanding of something. A child who is just starting school often wants to rely on learning, but there are many scholars who can't even eat and can't stop him from reading. Regarding this, some people may wonder, "Why do people 'like the new and dislike the old'?" I can answer that this is human curiosity. Curiosity can lead to interest, but curiosity has nothing to do with interest. An old gentleman goes to a dance floor to watch dancing entirely out of curiosity. If he says that he is interested in dancing because of this, then it is a wrong. Talking about the true meaning of his article to a person who has just recognized "zhiwu" will naturally give rise to the feeling of playing the piano to a cow; if he only has the strength to bear a weight of fifty catties, and he wants to make him carry a burden of one hundred catties, then he can only force people to walk on the road to death.

Based on the above explanation, it can be seen that it is not worth being surprised that Gu and Li cannot arouse interest in reading literary books, but there are actually their own reasons; due to the author's experience (such as the facts mentioned above), to solve this problem 丨Improve your interest in reading literary books, on the one hand, you need to make your life closer to literature, on the other hand, you must not think of "reaching the sky in one step" but learn that "step by step" step by step, of course, this is not an easy thing. (To be continued)

Beginning in the 23rd Year, Junior High Schools Must Implement Boy Scout Training

The Municipal Education Bureau Issued Instructions to All Schools Yesterday

The Municipal Education Bureau of this city, upon receiving instructions from the Ministry of Education, has directed that, beginning in the 23rd year [of the Republic, i.e., 1934], all public and private junior high schools should make Boy Scouting a required subject. The duration of study is set at three years, with three hours of instruction per week each year, one hour during class time and two hours outside of class time. All Boy Scout equipment expenses should be included in the school's budget as recurring expenses. After Boy Scouting is implemented in junior high schools, the Boy Scout uniform will become the school uniform for those schools, and there is no need to produce another uniform. As for primary school children, who are younger, Boy Scouting in primary schools should still be listed as extracurricular activities and need not be uniformly implemented during class time. The order has been forwarded to all public and private secondary schools that in the 23rd year, the junior high school departments of all secondary schools and junior high schools should universally provide Boy Scout training. Physical education teachers at each school should quickly enroll in Boy Scout instructor training classes to facilitate instruction. At the same time, the Education Bureau has sent a letter to the Shanghai Boy Scout Council, requesting them to organize a summer training class to enable physical education teachers from various schools to attend and learn.

The Municipal Education Bureau Urges Submission of Junior High School Graduation Exam Results

Deadline for Submission to the Bureau is the 18th of This Month

The Shanghai Municipal Education Bureau announced yesterday: "It has been determined that the graduation examinations for this year's secondary school students have been held on schedule. The graduation examination results of all secondary school students in this city who participated in the joint examination were previously required to be submitted to the Bureau by the 18th of this month for verification and record. As the deadline is imminent, you are hereby urged to promptly comply with the previous order and avoid delay. Failure to submit by the deadline will result in non-acceptance. This announcement is hereby issued."

The China Child Education Society's Record of Observation in Japan (9) Zhou Shang

1. National schools cultivate the foundation for the nation's ideals.

2. Social schools temper the practicalities according to the demands of society.

3. Children's schools guide children's lives and assist them in their upward progress.

Also observed were the school's three major characteristics: 1. strengthening physical fitness and emphasizing vocational guidance; 2. engaging in extracurricular guidance to enrich leisure life; 3. connecting with post-employment support organizations in vocational guidance.

The school views vocational guidance as the convergence point of the nation, society, and children, and as a necessary requirement of education, not merely a superficial and fashionable accessory. All aspects of play life and leisure life must have vocational guidance as their core. Vocational guidance is the result of holistic education. Therefore, true education awaits the reasonable combination and expression of both general cultivation and vocational guidance. Thus, vocational guidance is often linked to the entire education system. The following are some of the more obvious comparisons:

(1) Vocational Cultivation: To enable children to gain an understanding of occupations and practical skills, the children's mental attitude toward occupations must first be established. 1. Special instruction in learning guidance, training facilities, physical education, and health care. 2. Localization, pragmatism, and operationalization of various subjects. 3. Fellow student lectures, career talks, specimen collection. 4. Receiving guests and answering the phone in the school, practicing bicycle sales, connecting and unifying the guidance of various departments. 5. Diligent service, simulated employment, occupational participation, etc.

(2) Job Selection Guidance: With the goal of making the best use of talent, on the one hand, supervise children to work hard and make progress, so that they can adapt to the occupation, adapt to their personality, and adapt to the environment. 1. Various performance checks and overall observation. 2. Children's own reflection and occupational aspirations. 3. Reflection on circumstances and the hopes of parents. 4. Individual guidance on job selection and communication with the parents' association. 5. Job referrals and investigations. 6. Job placement and simulated employment.

(3) Post-Employment Counseling: Maintaining contact and counseling among the school, the individual, and society after employment. 1. Correspondence, visits, convening guidance. 2. Special establishment of a post-employment counseling department. 3. Alumni association, job love, alumni association magazines.

The above are all the school's claims. Some parts are worth adopting. After the visit, we were invited into the auditorium and served tea and snacks, and a movie about school life was shown. First, daily life was shown, such as school buildings, morning meetings, breaks, bugle calls, morning exercises, salutes, and various sports. Next, scientific life training was shown, such as research under a microscope, laboratory work, factory work, animal husbandry, and horticulture. Then, commercial practice was shown, such as remittance, counting tickets, typing, sales techniques, and exhibition products. Then, leisure life was shown, such as travel, cooking, etc. National spirit was shown, such as worshiping the hero Nan Gong, and social life was shown, such as boarding a boat for a visit. The lives of graduates were shown, such as chicks leaving the nest and serving in various places.

Looking at the spirit of the entire school, it is all focused on vocational education. According to the principal, 90% of the graduates over the years have jobs. At the end of March this year, more than a thousand people graduated, and most of them have already been employed. Among them, 305 are shop assistants, 340 are interns, 31 are going on to higher education, and 64 are others. Among the employed students, 373 were introduced by the school, 133 were introduced by their families, and 210 were introduced by others. "It is difficult to find a job in Japan now." According to a recent survey report, there are more than 29 million employed people and more than 34 million unemployed people in the country. Employed people only account for 45.6%, with men accounting for 59.1% and women accounting for 31.9%. Graduates of this school can easily find positions. If it were not for the proper training on weekdays, how could this achievement be possible?

The foundation of education in Japan today is labor training and military national education, which is its old foundation. Vocational education has reached an advanced goal. It is expected that factory-like schools and multi-faceted vocational education will be implemented. Japan, which is outwardly strong but inwardly weak, may be on par with the United States in less than twenty years. Their handicraft courses have remained handicraft courses for decades, unlike our country's handicraft courses, which have changed to crafts, then to labor, and other new terms. Observing the results, others are still far behind. Today, Japan can be said to have everyone educated (according to recent statistics, only two out of a thousand people have not received education). Therefore, even vendors and waiters are literate, and even maids have at least six years of primary school graduation qualifications.

He will practice at the Chinese Tennis Association every afternoon at 4 pm.

According to Tan, the Shanghai Tennis Association (formerly the Chinese Tennis Association) operated by Qiu Feihai, the land lease is completely free, and 10,000 yuan is used as the association's expenses. The clubhouse of the Chinese Tennis Association will be completed soon. It is also planned to build a three-story clubhouse on the back end of the red sand court when tennis sports are stopped in winter.
