Shanghai Racing Club's Ball Shooting Accuracy Competition Successfully Concluded. Ding Mingyi Champion of Group A, Xu Shizhang Runner-Up. Xu Baomin Champion of Group B, Yu Junfa Runner-Up

The second members' ball shooting accuracy competition initiated by the Shanghai Racing Club was held sequentially from the 1st of this month with great enthusiasm. The finals for Group A were held the night before last (the 14th). The competitors were Xu Shizhang, who is well-known in Shanghai, and Ding Mingyi, a rising star. Judging from their combat experience and skills, Xu was indeed formidable. Therefore, Zhuang Fengming and Fang Bofen, the impartial judges of the club in charge of this event, announced that Xu would have 800 points as the finish line, while Ding would have his points reduced to 620 as the finish line, so as to balance the strength of both sides. As a result, the audience was packed. Initially, Xu took the lead all the way. In the first 20 shots, he scored 276 points, far surpassing Ding's 93 points. The 180 points Xu gave Ding was a head start. Later, when Xu reached 400 points, Ding was still defeated, so everyone expected Xu to win easily. Unexpectedly, Ding suddenly had a smooth run, scoring many points in a row, step by step catching up, directly chasing little Xu, from close to even, and finally surpassing little Xu, winning with 620 points compared to Xu's 60 points, taking two and a half hours. The referee was Zhuang Fengming, and the recorder was Hu Yongan.

The Group B finals were also very interesting. Xu was a fledgling tiger, full of courage and vigor. Yu Junfa was a master, with excellent ball skills. Both were famous players. The difference in their balanced strength points was large. Xu had 215 points, and Yu had 420 points. Despite the difference, many still expected Yu to win steadily. During the competition, Yu once led by 200 points, but unexpectedly suddenly slumped, just like little Xu in Group A. The two were very similar, and Xu and Yu can be said to be in the same boat. In the end, when Xu reached the finish line in 25 minutes, Yu scored 391 points, taking two hours and five minutes. The referee was Jia Changhui, and the recorder was Qiu Yuanming.

The champions and runners-up of both Group A and Group B were each awarded a silver cup. After the Group A competition ended the night before last, Ms. Chen Zhaolu was respectfully invited by Lu Xiwu, the executive member of the club, to present the awards. The closing ceremony was then held amidst cheers and excitement.

The highest score in a single series of shots in each group in this competition was: Group A: Xu Shizhang with 61 points; Group B: Yu Junfa with 31 points.

Spring and Autumn

Records of Fragrant Incense Drifting

— Originally by Princess Der Ling of the Qing Dynasty, Translated by Qin Shouou

Once it comes to summer, we must wear gauze clothing as usual; So are we really wearing gauze clothes? Yes, we are really wearing gauze clothing! It's just that under the gauze, we specially make a layer of silk lining, and some cotton is stuffed in the middle. In this way, we can avoid violating the law on the one hand, and avoid being frozen on the other. However, this method is not a new invention, nor is it a secret, but an open compromise; Perhaps shortly after the formulation of these different clothes for the four seasons, someone came up with this method. Even the Empress Dowager herself often does the same. But because her position is so noble, the clothes she wears must always be more distinctive than others, so we use cotton, but she must use silk floss. Silk floss is a kind of messy silk that silkworms spit out. It has a higher temperature and lighter weight than cotton. It is also prepared by the silkworm-raising women in the palace specially for her, so of course it should be enjoyed by her.

Once April arrives, it is the beginning of spring, and all the female officials in the palace must wear jewelry ornaments together. All hairpins, earrings, rings, etc., are either strung with pearls or inlaid with jade, either jadeite or agate. Everyone is dressed in jewels and treasures, which is dazzling to the eye.

Readers can easily imagine how neat and uniform the clothing of officials and civilians in China under the rule of the Manchurian Qing Emperor was, after reading the above simple description; Although their politics were so corrupt, they did pay great attention to the appearance of clothing. Now let me talk more about women's clothing styles. Of course, women are more particular, simply because women love to dress up and love to follow the trend; Even if there are no legal regulations, they will definitely automatically create new styles. Therefore, when winter comes, all their clothing will be decorated with wintersweet flowers. (59)

The Study of Flying Men

— He Ru

In the history of Western mythology, the flying little fairies are stout, like five- or six-month-old babies, holding bows and arrows, with the image of wanting to shoot. There is also the flight of Apuchen Luo, without shadow or form. Holding a long spear in his hand, he pierced any part of the beauty's body. When her eyes first opened, all the first people she saw followed her to the death, unwilling to leave a step.

In Chinese novels, Wang Mang hired a giant on the sacred mountain, ten feet tall, with wings on his back, who could fly hundreds of miles and take the heads of generals as easily as taking things out of a bag. In the Battle of Kunyang, Ju Wuba flew up several times, but was struck down to the ground by thunderstorms. The last time, he desperately took off. Just when he reached Liu Xiu's head, there was a thunderbolt. Liu Xiu was unscathed, and Ju Wuba died in battle, so later history called it "Fengyu Zhan Kunyang" (Battle of Kunyang in Wind and Rain) because of this thunder.

When Hui Qin was besieged by the Jin soldiers, there was a team of six armored soldiers who could fly three feet high. Although it was not a rumor to confuse the public, it was of no help to saving the country. Hui Qin was captured, and the divine soldiers were disbanded. In "The Story of Yue Fei," it is also recorded that Niu Gao smashed the imperial wine to reward the army. The coachman died after drinking a cup, bleeding from all seven orifices. Niu Gao smashed it in anger, and not a drop remained. Although there was merit, it was really too reckless. He was expelled from the camp and had nowhere to go. He met a fairy who taught him piercing-cloud arrows, wave-walking shoes, and life-seizing pills. When attacking Chang Gong, the piercing-cloud arrows shot down a piece of Xi Yun and captured a flying demon. The wave-walking shoes captured Yang Gong. The life-seizing pill saved Yue Fei's life.

Is it true that someone can fly? A newspaper once drew a beautiful woman in its commemorative publication, driving a foot-powered flying machine and distributing newspapers in mid-air.

The "Art Life" magazine had six photos of flying men, blowing the carbon dioxide in their lungs into a rotary flying machine, which could then take off. The moment before taking off, flying as high as twelve meters above the ground, the upward view of thousands of revolutions, the situation of descending, and after safely landing, he told a reporter about his flying experiment: "This forty-second flight was like a dream."

Finger Painting

— Qia Qing

When finger painting originated is difficult to determine. In the past, Zeng Banshi and the servants of the First Emperor once painted water gods with their toes; Based on this inference, there should also be people who used their fingers to paint in the Zhou and Qin dynasties. Xiaoshan commented on painting: "Zhang Zao of the Tang Dynasty painted with his hands, and Bi Hong saw it and was surprised! When asked who taught him, he said: 'Externally, I take nature as my teacher, and internally, I obtain the source from my heart.'" Knowing that finger painting in the Tang Dynasty certainly existed, Qing Gao Qieyuan was also skilled in finger painting, calling it "finger life"; Figures, landscapes, birds, and fish were all vivid! Gao Bing of Liaodong once wrote a theory on finger painting: "Lord Keqin learned painting at the age of eight. Whenever he encountered a draft, he would stroke it. After more than ten years, he filled two baskets; When he reached adulthood, he regretted that he could not form his own style! Tired and drowsy, he dreamed that an old man led him to an earthen room. The four walls were covered with paintings, and all the theories were complete, but the room was empty, and he could not imitate them; Only a bowl of water, so he dipped his fingers and practiced with it; When he woke up, he was overjoyed! However, he could not apply what he had learned to the brush, so he was often depressed; He suddenly remembered the method of using water in the earthen room, so he dipped his fingers in ink and imitated the general outline, and obtained all its spirit; He could do whatever he wanted, and everything he did was perfect; Therefore, he abandoned the brush..." How could this truly be taught by the gods! It was because he had been painting for more than ten years, and his skills were already deep, and he suddenly realized something, so he could paint at will, which was the same mentality as the so-called "obtaining the source from the heart." As a result, finger painting stood out as a unique style in the Chinese painting world, and many virtuous scholars and officials playfully engaged in it.

Master Yan Ganyuan of the Late Evening Building, a senior in Guanzhong, is an expert in appraisal, rich in collections, good at calligraphy and painting; His calligraphy is exquisite in all styles, vigorous and ancient, and his reputation is well-known in the world; He mainly paints with his fingers, landscapes, figures, ladies, flowers, trees, fish, dragons, birds, and beasts. Once touched by his fingers, they are all vivid in spirit; And a kind of thick, majestic, and profound charm is especially beyond what the brush can achieve! Probably because Mr. grew up between the rivers and mountains, it is easy to obtain the help of the landscape from nature; Or because he is devoted to antiquities, and his cultivation is deep, he can handle things with ease, like this. I have never seen Zhang Zao's handwriting, so I dare not make any comparisons! If compared with what Ganyuan has done, then modern people are far better than the ancients. Mr. is seventy years old this year, and his spirit is hale and hearty, like a forty- or fifty-year-old man; He has recently created hundreds of finger paintings and calligraphy works, which will be displayed to the public at the Ningbo Fellow Association on the fifteenth, sixteenth, and seventeenth of this month. Those who read Mr.'s paintings in the world, wouldn't they be like Bi Hong seeing Zhang Zao?

Four Company Commanders of the Northeast

— Zhang Henshui

Chapter Thirty: Watching Sorrowful Geese Bury Their Heads to Defend the Country; Bullets Pierce Strong Arms and Sprinkle Blood to Stain the Lone City

Our heroes of the Republic of China have all conquered the east and the west in the past. Today, we are very polite to foreigners, but they treat us like this, can we endure this? At this time, there is nothing else to say, it is that they can take our lives, but not an inch of land can be taken away by others. It's like, you live at home, and you haven't offended anyone, but people can break into your house, can you say you won't fight back at all, and just sit here and let people beat you? All good kinds come. Let's close this door together, we can't let the enemy rush in. Do it, brothers. After Zi Qiang finished speaking, he raised the hoe with both hands and dug in the trench again. It was this exciting action of his that revived the lazy trend of the brothers. Zi Qiang thought to himself, no wonder our Battalion Commander Bao is so loyal and brave, it turns out there is a reason. A person who leads others, every move is related to all colleagues, and must be careful everywhere. A soldier must learn from our battalion commander. As soon as Zi Qiang turned his mind like this, he was originally supervising the work on the trenches, but now he did not supervise the work, but personally followed his brothers and dug in one place. But this kind of work is not an ordinary trench digging work. In the outer part of the pass, the weather is colder two months earlier than in the pass, and it is several times colder. At this time, it had already snowed several times. When the snow fell, it would never melt, and the mountains and valleys were all made of silver. Although the snow on the ground did not seep down, the cold air on the ground kept dropping several feet deep into the soil. As a result, some moisture in the soil was frozen into iron plates by the cold air. If you dig the hoe down, the soil can splash the hoe back. Fortunately, Bao Fang had already understood this difficulty in advance, and had already dug two trenches, and now it was just adding another one. (410)

Local Customs and Traditions

The Art of the Dragon Boat Festival

— Tiansheweng (Old Farmer)

A good festival of the year is a day of entertainment for the people. In times of peace and prosperity, when goods are abundant, good festivals and auspicious days are of course decorated with a lot of public entertainment, which cannot be said to be something that wastes people and money. Moreover, all the entertainment during the festival is not without consciousness, but it has been followed for a long time, and it has slowly lost its original meaning. Taking only the Dragon Boat Festival as an example, in terms of eating; Zongzi, loquats, green plums, shad, seasonal fresh fruits and delicacies are countless. Main entertainment: dragon boat races, hanging Zhong Kui, embroidered sachets, calamus swords and mugwort tigers, all kinds of things are very artistic, not only have a long history of value. The festival is in the middle of the sky, the wind is warm and the sun is warm, the flowers are blooming and the grass is growing, taking advantage of the time when the heat of summer has not yet arrived, talking about the story of the Dragon Boat Festival, isn't it a refreshing and happy thing?

(1) Zhong Kui It is said that Emperor Ming of Tang Dynasty suffered from malaria and dreamed of a big ghost, wearing a torn hat, a blue robe, a horn belt, and court boots, catching small ghosts and eating them. He claimed to be Zhong Kui, a scholar from Zhongnan, who had once taken the exam but failed, and died after touching the steps. Emperor Ming woke up from his dream and his illness was cured, so he ordered Wu Daozi to paint Zhong Kui's portrait. Later, the common people thought that the weather would gradually get hotter after the Dragon Boat Festival, and epidemics would come, thinking that ghosts and monsters were causing trouble. So on this day of the Dragon Boat Festival, they painted a portrait of Zhong Kui and hung it in the hall, thinking that it could scare away demons. In fact, Zhong Kui is the Zhong Kui in the "Records of Examination of Artisans", which is another name for a hammer. The ancients used hammers to drive away ghosts. Ma Rong's "Guangcheng Song" of waving Zhong Kui and raising jade axes is clear evidence. I don't know how, Emperor Ming came up with a Zhong scholar wearing a torn hat, blue robe, horn belt, and court boots, and asked Wu Daozi to paint it. Wu Daozi was a famous painter, and he was especially good at painting these ghosts and monsters, so of course he wrote very well. Zhong Kui is ugly, and his sister is beautiful. When ugliness and beauty are painted together, ugliness also becomes beauty. Therefore, the world has painted a picture of Zhong Kui marrying his sister, but it is very beautiful. Isn't the Dragon Boat Festival painting Zhong Kui an art?

(2) Dragon Boat Racing Liang Zonglin's "Chronicle of Jingchu" said: "Qu Yuan threw himself into the Miluo River on the fifth day of May, so Wuling used this day to race dragon boats to summon him." On this Dragon Boat Festival, there is a custom of dragon boat racing, which is more about advocating water sports than commemorating Qu Yuan. Because in the provinces of Hunan, Jiangxi, Zhejiang, Wu, and Hubei, rivers intersect, and the people are accustomed to playing in the water. The Dragon Boat Festival is also a season when the weather is warm, and it is most suitable for promoting water sports and encouraging martial spirit. Probably, the dragon boat racing was already promoted by King Fucha of Wu and King Goujian of Yue. Later generations followed suit and embellished, making the dragon boats gorgeous and exquisite, with drums and music, and the prows of the boats all dispatched. The ancient people's legacy of practicing naval warfare has also become artistic.

(3) Calamus Sword It is said that on the fifth day of May, there is a saying that the Tartars should be killed, because the Tartars regarded us Han people as slaves, raped women, and did everything. Our Han people hated it so much that they agreed to hang calamus and mugwort on the doors of every house on the fifth day of May as a sign, and everyone would rise up to kill all the Tartars. Although this legend is not very reliable, the matter of hanging calamus swords is still prevalent today, and there must be a reason for it. Probably, when the Jin and Yuan dynasties ravaged China, they were scattered everywhere. Relying on their own strength, they must have occupied people's fields, raped and looted, and they must retaliate for every grievance. Killing them was the only way to be happy. Hanging calamus swords and killing the Tartars, there may have been such a thing. The hearts of the people are not dead, and hegemony is difficult to last. Have we Chinese people forgotten the meaning of the ancients?

Shen Bao Radio Weekly

New Musical Instrument

— Li Yuanqing

There are many kinds of musical instruments made using vacuum tube low-frequency oscillators. One of the instruments introduced in this article, originally named Trautonium, was designed by Dr. Trautwein of Germany.

Figure 1

Figure 1 is a commonly used vacuum tube low-frequency oscillator. During oscillation, the frequency varies with the resistance and capacitance within the grid circuit. Because it is necessary to expand the range of frequency variation, both the capacitor and the resistor use relatively large values. When using, first turn the switch SW to set the volume, or to resonate with other instruments. Then, press the copper wire with your fingers to obtain different scales of pitch. (The exact position of each scale must be determined after experimentation.)

The structure of this device is very simple, and even people with no knowledge of radio can easily experiment according to the diagram. After completion, if no oscillation occurs, you can switch the two wire ends of the low-frequency transformer's primary coil (the secondary coil can also be switched). If this still doesn't work, then the inside of the vacuum tube is damaged and needs to be revived or replaced with a new tube.

Figure 2

Furthermore, according to actual experimentation, the use of a triode vacuum tube is most effective. As for the type, both AC and DC vacuum tubes are acceptable.

The materials required for this device and their values are as follows:

C2 = .5mf V = 3o vacuum tube

C3 = .25mf R = 2o ohm variable filament regulator

C4 = .Imf RI = five-section wire-wound fixed resistor

Simple AC Voltage Controller

— Yizhi

In the city's power supply, the voltage often fluctuates day and night due to the different power consumption of users. The voltage fluctuation has a great impact on the radio's reception; Moreover, excessively high voltage can cause the vacuum tube to break, or the screen current to be too large and damage it. Therefore, it should be controlled to prevent accidents. Now, a simple and economical AC voltage controller is introduced. The method is simple, and comrades who love radio can make it themselves. Please refer to the attached diagram. Wind forty turns of No. 16 double yarn-covered wire densely on a bakelite tube (it is better to apply a layer of varnish on the coil to increase insulation). Connect one end of the two wire ends to the transformer and the other end to the power supply. Then, use a soft iron rod of appropriate size, or a long screw nut nail can also be used, and insert it into the bakelite tube. If the external voltage drops, remove the iron rod; If the external voltage rises, insert the iron rod, so that this simple device completes the work of the choke coil. The number of turns of the coil is not necessarily limited to forty turns, depending on how the local voltage changes; It can be less than forty turns, or more than forty turns, or connect the center tap. In short, adjust the appropriate voltage to keep the secondary coil voltage of the power transformer at a constant specified value, so that the radio's reception is satisfactory and the vacuum tube is not damaged.

Distortion

— Wu Shanchang

Apart from specially designed radios in high-rise buildings, distortion is a very common phenomenon in radios made by amateur enthusiasts. Radio operators do not need to pay attention to this phenomenon, but amateurs must pay attention if they want to improve the sound quality.

So let's first ask: is the radio stable? If there is a high-frequency amplification stage, does it tend to oscillate when turned to a radio station? This unpleasant high-pitched "hissing" sound makes the music turn into a whistling and hurried sound.

The modification method is to modify the high-frequency amplification stage or add a shielding cover, but simply rearranging the component layout, such as the coil angle and main wiring, will do. The instability of high-frequency amplification is only a problem of layout and position design, not due to a special state.

It is impossible for the coil and capacitor in the high-frequency amplification stage to still be unstable after using a shielding cover.

Distortion is more common in the low-frequency amplification than in the high-frequency amplification.

When using two stages of low-frequency amplification, or using a pentode as the output in the final stage, it is best to use resistance coupling.

Vacuum tube overload can also cause distortion, and incorrect B voltage is also a reason.

Each vacuum tube must have its correct plate voltage and grid voltage, so the instructions specified in the instruction manual must be noted. A certain B voltage should use a certain C voltage to save plate power and the sound is clear.

If the B voltage of the vacuum tube is sufficient, it is also necessary to pay attention to whether the C voltage can work. Ordinary C voltage can last for six to eight months (referring to foreign batteries, domestic products cannot be used for so long in comparison). Otherwise, use a meter to measure it before using it.

Excessive output can also cause distortion, so only reduce its volume or use a vacuum tube with a larger output power. In other words, use a powerful tube instead. The C voltage value used for this type of vacuum tube is higher, so the plate current also increases accordingly.

Many amateurs tend to use high-ratio transformers. This hope is sometimes hit hard because the amplification efficiency has a certain limit before it is stable without distortion. Therefore, it is better to use a lower ratio for low-frequency amplification with two-stage transformer coupling.

For low-frequency amplification with two transformer couplings, grounding the transformer core and appropriately spacing the wiring positions can prevent instability.

Inferior transformers also have poor frequency characteristics, which often cause distortion. Therefore, it is best to use cheap goods less.

As for using a three-circuit regenerative radio or excessive regeneration, excessive B voltage can also easily cause distortion. At that time, just reduce the B voltage or reduce the regeneration to prevent it.

If amateurs can pay attention to the above points, the drawbacks of distortion can be avoided.

Obtaining Ether

— Ming Xiang

Radio waves must have a medium for propagation in the air. This medium is hypothetically named "ether" in radio science. However, the so-called ether is completely a hypothetical term. There is no way to answer what its shape and nature are. Even whether it exists is still a question. Countless great scientists have exhausted their brains and done tens of millions of experiments to prove the existence of this ether and express its characteristics, but they have ultimately failed.

Recently, Professor Vaclavposjpa of Prague University in the capital of Czechoslovakia is confident that he has obtained the fleeting image of ether. He imagines that ether must contain a large group of atomic particles, similar to the central nucleus of oxygen atoms, but without charge. He once placed a thin wire made of steel (one of the metal elements) in a completely vacuum tube, and tried to heat it, and its resistance can be measured before and after heating. The experimental results showed that the oxygen nuclei in the tube dispersed and gathered on the palladium wire. Professor Pospěch is convinced that this stored particle is ether. Professor AimeCotton of the University of Paris also said that ether can be obtained by dispersing water molecules in a vacuum.

Improvement of a New Type of Power-Saving Single-Tube Machine

— Ma Xixian

I am most interested in experimenting with new vacuum tubes, so after reading Si Lianjun's single IA6 tube machine in the last issue, I immediately went to get one to try. As a result, the volume was of course louder, but the sensitivity and selectivity were still not satisfactory, so after many disassembly and reassembly, I changed it to a single-tube three-use machine with one stage of high-frequency amplification, one stage of detection, and one stage of low-frequency amplification. Its performance is really amazing. When receiving large and small radio stations in this city, almost no antenna is needed, so it is best to install it in a suitcase as a travel machine.

Parts list

CIC2 are all ○○○ four six variable capacitors C3 ○○○ two five grid capacitor C4 is a small ○○○ three five variable capacitor for adjusting regeneration C5C6 are all ○○ two bypass capacitors

R two MEO grid leak RI variable filament resistance T is a low-frequency transformer

RFC high-frequency choke coil

V is IA6 vacuum tube

Six-pin tube socket one

Pocket AC Radio

— Wang Caiwen

This so-called pocket radio is not small enough to be hidden in a pocket, but its size can be said to be much smaller than any small radio in the past.

When I started designing this radio, my goal was to minimize it as much as possible, and I didn't have time to consider efficiency, but the result was unexpectedly beautiful, so I especially introduce it here.

Because the purpose of this radio is to be small, all vacuum tubes are the latest type. Secondly, if ordinary variable capacitors are used, they will take up a lot of space, so new variable capacitors are used. This new variable capacitor has a capacitance of 0.00033, a thickness of only 15 mm, and a width of 63 mm, which is much smaller than before.

The branch capacitor is an 8uf electrolytic type. The low-frequency choke coil used in the filter is not used, but a German-style resistor is used instead. The detection uses a No. 57 industrial tube, which has very good efficiency when used for grid detection at low voltage, and the current consumption is small. The list of parts used in the whole machine is as follows:

Coil

L1 25 turns on a one-inch cylinder

L2 115 turns of 30 gauge enameled wire

L3 415 turns

Capacitors (unit uf)

VC1 VC2 new variable capacitor as mentioned above Co·ooo25 grid capacitor C2o·oo1 C3o·1 C4o·o1 C51·o

C68·o C72·o C88·o

Resistors (unit ohms)

R1 500,000 to 2 meg

R2 2 meg to 3 meg

R3 300,000 to 500,000

R4 1 meg to 2 meg

R6 50,000 R7 30,000 RCH 1 omh

RT secondary winding

200 volts 30 amps

5 volts 0.5 amps

2.5 volts 3 amps

V1 UZ57

V2 UY27A or UY227A

V3 KX12B

If you use 227B instead of V2 27A, although the efficiency is better, its shape is slightly larger, so it is sometimes inconvenient to use.

Adjustment and sensitivity

The thing that feels uneasy when looking at this circuit is the problem of AC hum, because C6 and C8 have large capacitance, and the values of R6 and R7 are too large, so the AC hum caused by ripple is not a problem. What must be noted is the AC hum caused by induction. The initial experiment felt very annoying. When the earpiece was hanging on the ear, the oh-oh sound occurred terribly. Later, after various changes, this noise was finally eliminated.

The sensitivity is quite good. It is really amazing that such a small radio can be heard so clearly. Readers may wish to try it.

Yesterday's flour market, although foreign wheat was small after the opening of the market in the morning, because the flour exchange was closed for two days, the floating households rushed to make up for it. The market has been standing since the opening of the market. Then there were money shops to buy distant futures, and the market stepped up. In the afternoon, Mingyue continued to stand up. Only in September, a large factory sold off, and the factory's limit price was 2.09 yuan, so it was never able to break through the price of 2.09 yuan or more. In other months, there were non-industry speculators and empty buyers, and they all saw the rise. The closing prices in June and August rose by 0.0125, July and October rose by 0.01, November rose by 0.015, and September was only half a point.

Early Wheat Morning Soft Noon Back

In the afternoon, there was an opportunity to make up for the empty position, and then the opportunity began, but the closing prices of distant months were still a little 0.01 each, and the recent ones had no ups and downs. Silk and Tea New Cocoons Transported to Shanghai Silk Factory Opens

(25 Factories Have Arrived in Shanghai) There were originally 113 single and double palace silk factories in Shanghai. In recent years, overseas silk sales have plummeted, and silk prices have plummeted. Factories that went bankrupt are frequently heard of. Before the new cocoons were launched, only 11 or 12 factories worked hard. This year, Jiangsu and Zhejiang spring silkworms have reported a bumper harvest. Improved seed cocoons are of good quality and the price is not high. The cocoon market ended one after another. New dry cocoons were transported to Shanghai one after another. Each silk factory in the city has started work one after another. Now 25 factories in Shanghai have started running, including Yunchang, Yichang 1.2.3, Zhengda, Jiyu, Gongda, Fengji, Yuanji, Fuchang, Yutong, Gongji, Fengtai, Fulunheng, Xuxing, Xianglun, Yufeng, Tongyi, Tongwei, Jinyun, and Chuxin. There are still several factories such as Baotai and Xinchang. They are currently repairing locomotives and will start work within a few days.

(Overseas Factory Price Survey) In the overseas market, Japanese silk merchants actively sold cheap Japanese new silk, resulting in extremely sluggish Chinese silk market. The current market price of Grade B white factory warp, "New York" 80% evenness, 20 to 22 yarns is only 456 to 460 yuan. "Lyon" 13 to 15 yarns is only 520 to 530 yuan. The cost of new silk for each manufacturer is 550 to 560 yuan. It is difficult to sell at a loss, and the Shanghai market is still stalled.

(Double Palace Silk Indian Demand Still Strong) Recently, the demand for double palace silk printing is still strong. Previously, there was also 23 packs of double palace silk exported on the British mail ship Laval Soldier Brothers, which was transported to India via the UK.

(Electro-transferred Factory Warp Price Still Small) In the European and American raw silk market, the current silk factory entry is still sluggish, and silk prices are hovering. Although each European bank received an overseas account yesterday morning, the white factory warp price is still small. The negotiations between Chinese and foreign parties are still suspended by 40 to 50 yuan, and it is difficult to comply. Yesterday, the silk factory entered 5 packs each of yellow factory warp and white dry warp, and the price was still flat and weak.

Free Talk

Snacks

— Mo Zhen

The current state of the publishing industry, with many periodicals and few specialized books, makes those with a heart worry, and many small pieces and few great works also make those with a heart worry. People with a heart really have to "sit in the city of sorrow" every day.

However, this situation has been going on for a long time, and now it is only slightly changed and more obvious.

The residents of Shanghai have always liked to eat snacks. If you listen carefully, the snack vendors outside the house are always "really busy". Osmanthus white sugar London cake, lard white sugar lotus seed porridge, shrimp meat wonton noodles, sesame bananas, Nanyang mangoes, West Road honey oranges, melon seed kings, as well as candied fruits, olives, etc., etc., as long as you have a good appetite, you can eat from morning to midnight, but it doesn't matter if you don't have a good appetite, because it's not like fatty fish and big meat, and the portion is very small. The effect is that in leisure, you get the benefits of Lilian, and the taste is good.

The publications of the past few years are snacks that "benefit health", or "introduction", or "ABC", or "overview". In short, it is a thin book, as long as you spend a few cents and spend half an hour, you can understand a kind of science, or a complete literature, or a kind of foreign language. The meaning is that as long as you eat a pack of five-spice melon seeds, you can make this person flourish and grow, which is worth eating for five years. After trying it for a few years, the effect was not obvious, so I felt a little discouraged. If the test is inconsistent with the name, it is often inevitable to be discouraged. For example, there are now very few people who practice immortality or refine gold, and instead use Haoquan and buy lottery tickets, which is the result of ineffective testing. So it was released. The "health" side has been moved to the "taste good" side. Naturally, snacks are still snacks. Residents of Shanghai cannot be separated from snacks even if they die.

So small pieces appeared, but it was not a new pattern. When the business of Lao Jiuzhang was booming, there was a "Grand View of Notes and Novels", which was a large box of snacks; after Lao Jiuzhang closed, it naturally became a small pinch. The portion is smaller, so why is it so noisy and raging, causing a storm in the city? I think this is because a signboard with a seal character and a Roman alphabet combined with a New Year red electric light is installed on the load.

However, although it is still a snack, the Shanghai residents' sensitivity is more agile than before, otherwise why would it be noisy? But this may be due to neurasthenia. If so, then the future of snacks is worrying.

What is Literary Chinese?

— Cao Qiren

"…Once vernacular Chinese becomes popular throughout the country, and everyone can use writing to express their ideas to some extent, then the extraordinary skills that the scholar class has always possessed will have no place to be used… The popularization of Chinese characters, on the one hand, provides the people with a new tool to express their thoughts, allowing tens of millions of previously silent people to express their simple ideas after learning three to five hundred characters; on the other hand, it deprives the scholar class of their only weapon… It is not without awareness that the old gentlemen oppose vernacular Chinese; it is precisely their last struggle, the final brilliance of their lives."

丨丨Tao Menghe: The Scholar Class Someone told me: "'Literary Chinese Revival', 'Elementary School Classics', there are people advocating, echoing, the noise is deafening, the restoration movement is really afraid it will become a reality," I smiled without answering, and asked him to show me the articles of the advocates. I said: What they themselves do, can it be considered Literary Chinese? The world is so bizarre, those who yearn for Literary Chinese, their illness lies in not understanding at all "what is Literary Chinese?" This kind of "New Citizen Journal" style of writing, not only would the orthodox Tongcheng school disdain it, even seeds of culture must shake their heads and sigh at it as a great calamity for the world and people's hearts (see Kang Youwei and Liang Qichao), and they are complacent thinking that what they do is Literary Chinese, isn't that a big joke! Just saying that advocating Literary Chinese revival is stubborn and conservative is not enough to convince their hearts, I will calmly talk about the so-called "essence of Literary Chinese". I think, those who advocate Literary Chinese revival should adhere to the Tongcheng school's claims, that is their old master. Among the four disciples of Yao Nai of the Tongcheng school, Fang Dongshu was the most cautious, let's see what he said: "The writing of the three dynasties gradually declined in style, the times made it so. Moreover, in recent times, ancient teachings are rarely understood, rather than writing in a way that people do not understand, why not use what is commonly understood and make it easy to understand?" (Explanation of the Book Forest) Under Zeng Guofan's command, Wu Jifu (Rulun) had the highest attainment in learning ancient prose, let's listen to his argument: "China cannot popularize education without abolishing Han Chinese; because Han Chinese is too difficult, people learn it from a young age, and it is impossible to become refined and admirable without decades of hard work, and by then people are old and useless, this is why our country's scholarship is not as advanced as the West." Mr. Xu Binbin said it well: "People are neither new nor old, as long as they are clear about the principles of things, they will naturally have a fair and pertinent argument." Those who love to drive backwards are mostly ignorant fools who forget their ancestors and do not understand the principles of things!

Opposing "Literary Chinese" and "Vernacular Chinese", thinking that the two are absolutely incompatible; they think they have seized that camp, raised the banner, and opposed the Vernacular Chinese camp, this is the root of all wrong ideas. Language and writing are produced in the community, used in the community, and are always in a constant process of change and selection, trying to intercept the language of a certain time and place, calling it Literary Chinese, calling it ancient Chinese, that is absolutely impossible. Liu Zhifan said: "As time passes, customs are impermanent, later generations will look at the present as the present looks at the past; but writers are all afraid to write in the language of today, and bravely imitate the language of the past, isn't that a delusion!" He also said: "The theories of the Three Commentaries are not familiar with the Book of Documents, and the words of the Han Dynasty often contradict the strategies of the Warring States, enough to verify the gradual changes in popular customs, and to know the differences in the times. But later writers have no foresight, record the spoken language of their time, rarely write truthfully, and then imitate the people of the past, showing their antiquarianism. This makes the language of the Zhou and Qin dynasties appear in the Wei and Jin dynasties, and the responses of the Chu and Han dynasties are used in the Song and Qi dynasties, falsely repairing chaos, losing their naturalness, the present and the past are impure because of this, and the true and the false are confused by their mutual mixing. We use a historical perspective to observe the changes in language and writing, and we know that the words "Literary Chinese" cannot be established at all, what they are based on is a dreamlike state, there is no actual camp, what can they use to oppose "Vernacular Chinese"!

Originally, Chinese language and writing took the Qin Dynasty as a dividing line. Before the Qin Dynasty, various ethnic groups managed their own cultures and used their own dialects to write articles, what is called ancient Zhou and Qin writings today, were in fact dialect writings at the time. To describe the beauty of a person, the Shanghai dialect is "pretty", using it in writing, those who advocate Literary Chinese always think it is too vulgar, and must change it to "graceful" or "beautiful" to be ancient and elegant. But the Erya says: "Graceful, beautiful. Between Song, Wei, Jin, and Zheng is called beautiful, between Chen, Chu, Zhou, and South is called graceful." It is precisely the dialect of that time; must abandoning "pretty" and take "beautiful" or "graceful", isn't that knowing two fives but not knowing one ten? Early people's affairs are simple, and characters were first used to describe meaning with one character (same as foreign tribes, East is called Yi, West is called Rong, South is called Man, North is called Di). As human affairs gradually become complicated, the number of characters increases day by day, which is very difficult to remember, and naturally tends towards the new path of using words. The tendency to use words gradually sprouted between the Zhou and Qin dynasties, and became more obvious after the Han Dynasty, single characters were abandoned and compound words rose again, from simple to complex, the trend is inevitable. Since the Han and Jin Dynasties, the increase in compound words is directly proportional to the times, and vernacular Chinese is purely using compound words. What those who advocate Literary Chinese yearn for is nothing more than the simplicity of using single characters in ancient times, but they do not know that the ancients were suffering from the inadequacy of simplicity! Yuan Zhonglang's Snow Waves Pavilion Preface says: "The ancient times had their own times, and the present times have their own times. To imitate the traces of ancient people's language and think it is ancient is like wearing summer clothes in severe winter." Yuan Boxiu's Essay on Collecting Bai Su says: "The round-collared robe of today is to learn from the ancient people's covering themselves with leaves. Today's five-flavored decoction is to learn from the ancient people's eating raw meat and drinking blood. The ancient people's intention was to satisfy their hunger and cover their bodies, and today's people's intention is also to satisfy their hunger and cover their bodies, there is no difference. Those who pick ancient people's words and phrases to put into their own works are no different from sewing leaves into their sleeves or throwing hair into the meat. Generally speaking, the writing of the ancients was dedicated to being clear, while the writing of today's people is dedicated to being unclear, learning to be clear from being unclear, can this be called learning from the ancients? Their words are the right medicine for those who advocate Literary Chinese revival!

Those who advocate Literary Chinese must speak highly of ancient Han and Wei prose, praising Sima Qian to the skies. If they were in Sima Qian's time, they should at least revive the writing of the Yin and Zhou Dynasties. But when Sima Qian wrote the Basic Annals of the Five Emperors, he translated the Shang Shu's "sincerely ordering the hundred officials, and the many achievements are all glorious" into "sincerely admonishing the officials, all the achievements are flourishing." Isn't that abolishing Literary Chinese and using Han Dynasty vernacular? Gao Yao said: "The people are submerged in darkness, I ride in four vehicles, follow the mountains to cut wood, and give to the Qin people fresh food." Isn't that simple and ancient, but the Historical Records' Basic Annals of Xia must change it to "The people are all afflicted by the water, I travel on land by carriage, travel on water by boat, travel on mud by sled, travel on mountains to cut wood and give to my people, so that the people have rice and fresh food." Isn't that abandoning simplicity for complexity, admitting that the language of today is superior to the language of the past? Those who advocate Literary Chinese must admire Han Yu, Liu Zongyuan, Ouyang Xiu, and Su Shi, thinking that the ancient prose of the Tang and Song dynasties is completely beautiful and perfect. Han Yu's Epitaph for Fan Shaoshu says: "Only by being ancient can one necessarily be strange, and those who descend cannot be strange. Song Qi liked ancient characters, and Ouyang Xiu leisurely slept and recorded auspicious signs, Zhalan Hong teased him with eight characters." The ancient prose writers of the Tang and Song dynasties were critical of the literati of the time for liking to use ancient language (just as people today like to use Literary Chinese), artificially creating, so they replaced it with "plain writing" (the name ancient prose was created by the people of the Ming Dynasty. The literati of the Tang and Song dynasties all called it plain writing, plain writing is plain and clear writing, just like novels have plain speech). If Han Yu and Liu Zongyuan were to be reborn in this world, they would definitely denounce the revival of Literary Chinese as... Those who advocate Literary Chinese must follow the Tongcheng school, and the Tongcheng school takes Gui Youguang as its ancestor, before Fang and Yao, there were Gu Tinglin and Wei Xi and others who continued it. Gu Tinglin's Daily Knowledge Records' criticism of literati seeking ancient ways says: "The Post Zhou Book's Biography of Xiong Tuo says: 'People at that time discussed the difference between ancient and modern styles of writing, Tuo thought that "times have ancient and modern, not writing has ancient and modern." This is the most appropriate argument. It is like the Han cannot do Shang. To copy or imitate the way of the Han Dynasty to replace... the two words of... in writing, is particularly inappropriate. To consider today's land as not ancient, and to borrow ancient land names; to consider today's officials as not ancient, and to borrow ancient official names; to abandon the commonly used characters of today, and to borrow the commonly used things of ancient times, are all ways for literati to exhaust their vulgarity." I don't know what those who advocate Literary Chinese revival think after reading it? What makes Gui Youguang different from the Seven Masters Before and After is that the Seven Masters Before and After intended to make fake antiques, failing to draw a tiger, becoming clumsy instead: Gui Youguang started with being plain and approachable, and unexpectedly entered a better state. The Tongcheng school advocates using the elegant words of the scholar-official class, and must use the current system for times and places, officials and institutions, focusing the collection and commentary of large and small chapters on one central point, its intention is to correct the mistakes of the restoration concepts of the Seven Masters Before and After, to make it easier for those who study writing to understand, and to adapt to the times, how can one "live in today's world" and practice the ways of the ancient world? The above discussion is all old news, it was unnecessary to say it again. I am only like a teacher who has taken in a few inferior students, repeatedly instructing them earnestly, hoping that they will neither mislead themselves, nor mislead the people of the world. Most importantly, they should understand that there is no such thing as Literary Chinese, they should not dream anymore, or talk in their sleep! (Adu, Ningxin, old literati called Literary Chinese writing; these are all earthy words of the Jin people (Adu) is like saying (this), "Ningxin" is like saying "like this". Historical Records, describes Zhou Bo's stuttering, so it says: "Your subject thinks it is impossible again and again," old literati then used "thinks it is impossible again and again" as Literary Chinese. The sage said, to know is to know, to not know is to not know, this is knowledge, those who don't understand what Literary Chinese is, better keep your mouth shut!)

Gejiu Mine (Part 2)

— Li Qiao

The cave is very stuffy, and with each person going in to carry ore, with a burning gas lamp stuck in their head, the air in the cave is almost entirely thick carbon gas, and by the time they carry the ore out, their faces have turned pale and they are panting heavily, throwing the two heavy bags of ore onto the ground, and leaning against the carrying pole as if they are about to die.

I was stunned when I saw this pitiful sight. I, a twelve or thirteen-year-old child, have come all the way here away from my parents, isn't it also to do this inhuman work?

I felt sad and wanted to cry, but I didn't dare. I silently followed the "water carrier" acquaintance, from this gang's shack to that gang's shack, stepping on piles of ore, walking past with a rustling sound.

On the way, he told me that those who carry ore are doing "grass skin work", and those who climb into the cave are "off-shift"...

"Do you want to do grass skin work? Or off-shift?" he suddenly asked me. "Those who do grass skin work have to carry all day, those who are off-shift only need to carry enough a few buckets of ore a day. Which do you prefer?"

I was afraid and didn't answer him.

He led me to a shack in Huazhakou. A big black dog rushed towards us fiercely, but was stopped by the people in the shack. The dogs here are mostly so fierce, the "water carrier" acquaintance said.

After eating in the shack, (the rice was coarse rice mixed with sand and gravel, the only dish was a pot of "Old Mother Soup") the "water carrier" acquaintance introduced me to the boss, and also said that I could work off-shift, and the wages were negotiable…

The boss looked at me over his pipe and chuckled: "Okay, you can learn tomorrow!"

After the boss said that, I felt a different kind of sadness in my heart!

That night, I hid under the blanket, without letting anyone know, and quietly shed a few tears of sorrow!

This place is a living hell: with inhuman cruelty, tyrannical exploitation, and dark oppression. If I hadn't come here, how would I have known?

Guiying's Dad (2)

— Yezi

So I didn't go downstairs much. Whenever my wife and they had nothing to say or do, I would go to bed and sleep, temporarily leaving the loneliness outside the mosquito net.

After half a month of this, I discovered Guiying's dad as if I had found a treasure.

I had known about Guiying's dad for a long time. Guiying and my wife's two elder sisters were classmates and very good friends, and they were also neighbors. Guiying's house was only separated from the hotel by two other houses. Guiying married a Nanjing man and lived in Shanghai. Only her elderly father and mother were left at home. Her mother was friends with my mother-in-law, and the reason why my mother-in-law was willing to marry her youngest daughter to me, this "outsider", was decided after being persuaded by Guiying's mom. Therefore, Guiying's mom often treated us as benefactors, telling us not to forget her. On this point, I was certainly grateful to her, but in fact, I had more hatred than gratitude for her. She was very ugly, with sparse hair, disheveled and uncombed. One of her eyes was blind, but that one lonely bright eye held a lot of fierceness, as if it had also combined the fierceness that the blind eye should have. Her face was yellow with a hint of green, but it was matched with a blood-basin-like big mouth, in which there was only one upper incisor. She bared this dagger-like incisor, specializing in cursing the streets and stirring up trouble. People on half a street had a wary attitude towards her. She didn't laugh often, but when she laughed, her mouth opened wider, her incisor was more exposed, and her appearance became more terrifying. Her left hand was numb, and she always had her right hand supporting it. There was also something wrong with her feet, and she walked with a limp. She always wore a set of dirty and smelly black clothes, which made people sick. All of this made her into a ghostly figure. Only my mother-in-law was quite close to her, and believed her words. Other than that, no one had a good impression of her.

Not only outsiders, but even her own daughter, Guiying, had a very bad feeling towards her. Guiying was a capable woman. She worked outside, and always sent more than ten dollars a month to her parents' home, but her good intentions were very painful. Once, we met her in Shanghai, and when we talked about the situation at home, she said sadly:

"It's very difficult for me. It's not good not to send this money, and it's not good to send it either. I originally wanted to send the money to my dad for him to use. My dad has always treated me well, and he is too hardworking and too pitiful. He is over sixty years old, and he is still selling sesame cakes and kudzu starch jelly, and ever since my brother passed away, he has been mourning so much that he has almost gone crazy, and he has become terribly decadent. Now his only hope is me, I must comfort him... I send ten dollars a month, and he could have stopped doing business. However, my mom is really too greedy. She hides all the money I send, and doesn't give a penny to my dad. She still forces my dad to do business. She knows how to enjoy herself very well, and she can't eat without fish and meat every day, but she doesn't let my dad enjoy it with her, leaving him only bones and soup. This situation is really tragic to talk about! Sometimes, I can't stand it and want to stop sending money. I remember how my mother used to mistreat me. When I lost my job, she didn't even allow me to eat a mouthful of rice at home, forcing me to go outside. Fortunately, I had good luck and got help from my friends, and I actually graduated from high school, married a husband, and now I also have a profession. All of this I earned with my own bare hands, what kindness have my parents shown me? Just because my dad is too pitiful, I want to do my duty to him, who knew that in the end my dad still hasn't benefited from my good intentions, but has been taken advantage of by my cruel mother, then isn't my money being spent too unjustly? What's the point of sending it anymore? However, when I think carefully, if I don't send money, my mother will definitely treat my dad even worse, then my dad will suffer even more. It's always for my dad's sake that I still send the money to my mother every month..."

When I lived at my mother-in-law's house, I didn't know about these situations yet. At that time, I only knew that Guiying's mom was an old annoyance, and that she and her husband were very miserable. Guiying's dad sold kudzu starch jelly under the city gate, and you could see him from the hotel entrance. He was a bald and short old man. I had also seen him come to the hotel to buy wine a few times. When he saw me, he always smiled and nodded, without saying a word, took the wine, silently paid the money, and left. I had to eat some snacks every afternoon, and although the street was deserted, there were often people selling noodles and kudzu starch jelly passing by. Once, I was waiting at the hotel entrance when Guiying's dad suddenly brought a large bowl of kudzu starch jelly and asked me to eat it. Kudzu starch jelly was something I originally liked, but I didn't dare to accept what he sold. Because when I saw his kudzu starch jelly, I would associate it with the appearance of Guiying's mom and the appearance of their small, dark house. This association made me want to vomit even when looking at the bowl of kudzu starch jelly.

Fortunately, that time A Ren helped me out and finished that big bowl. But from then on, I only ate noodles, and didn't buy kudzu starch jelly from others. If I bought kudzu starch jelly from others, Guiying's dad would definitely still see it, which would be too embarrassing.

I heard my wife and them say that Guiying's dad had a son who had been a standing committee member of the county party department during the revolutionary era, and was later shot. Since then, Guiying's dad's nerves had been a little strange. Sometimes he would remain silent, finish his business, and sit in the corner of his house, crying, and sometimes he would erupt, and then speak nonsense, wave his hands and feet, and make a big scene on the street.

My knowledge of Guiying's dad's situation was only this. But in the first half month, I had not seen him "erupt" once, probably that time was the silent period.
